
-----title
吉安（吉州） (出生地)
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1233&endYear=1237')">1233-1237年</a>　居乡庐陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1240')">1238-1240年</a>　入蒙学，受业朱植、曾深甫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年</a>　入白鹭洲书院，从欧阳守道学；又从王泰来学诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年</a>　本年父良佐死。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1243')">1242-1243年</a>　白鹭洲书院读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　赴童子试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1252')">1245-1252年</a>　居乡庐陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　本年与邓光荐开始交往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1256')">1254-1256年</a>　居乡庐陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　儿子将孙生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年6月17日</a>　庐陵乡里长老八十六岁生日，有贺词。作品：《青玉案》（里中上大人谁大）<div id='poem_91089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青玉案<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>寿老登八十六岁，戊午六月十七日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1258年6月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91089")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91089'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91089'>里中上大人谁大。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91089'>人上大、仁难作。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91089'>八十六翁闲处坐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91089'>小生懒惰，近来高卧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91089'>忘却今朝贺。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91089_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91089'>甲申还是连珠么。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91089'>剩有老人星一个。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91089'>白发朱颜堪婆娑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91089'>灵光殿火，昆明劫过。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91089'>角绮园黄我。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_91089_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年</a>　本年秋，与庐陵同县人王寿鹏、曾应龙举于乡。辰翁居魁。廷对被斥。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年</a>　居乡庐陵。福州人陈俞来吉作节度推官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年</a>　结交吉州推官陈俞。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='132c718f3460408193d6e4ffc031f613_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("132c718f3460408193d6e4ffc031f613");'><span id='132c718f3460408193d6e4ffc031f613_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>，32岁</div><div id='132c718f3460408193d6e4ffc031f613' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　居庐陵，为入沅的郭德章作序。作品：《郭德章序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（该序文今不存，据刘将孙《送郭士石序》）</span><div id='poem_1319249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319249?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郭兼山冲晦中庸说序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1263年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319249")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319249'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319249'>吾党纤悉物理，欲如白黑多寡而后能喻，至言天人性命之际，往往愈析愈离，而真实愈不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319249_comment'></div>此《中庸》所以有伐柯睨视之叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319249_comment'></div>旧爱先儒释中，以为一家则堂为中，一厅则堂非中，而厅自有中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319249_comment'></div>物理不可谓不极也，然尝小年观月，见其若步相随人，而不知其体之未尝动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319249_comment'></div>长而游四方，观于星垣斗极，虽极南极北万里之远，而目前者犹是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319249_comment'></div>由是悟所谓中无不在者，又非一处自有一中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319249_comment'></div>是理也，尝言于人，而未尝言于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319249_comment'></div>尝言于人者无隐乎尔，未尝言于人者日用而不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319249_comment'></div>新淦尹真定何君示予以郭兼山父子《中庸说》，将刊布之，求序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319249_comment'></div>余开卷即得其大者，了与人意无异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319249_comment'></div>其言曰：「天地之数起于中合，中合之变起于自然，而不可推移，故民受天地之中以生，所谓命也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319249_comment'></div>又曰：「孟子言不失赤子之心，此得天命之性者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319249_comment'></div>又曰：「必有事焉，则上天之载可以驯致，或萌于心，或感于事，隐而未见，朕而未发，皆所谓谨独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319249_comment'></div>然则谨独之道何为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319249_comment'></div>先儒谓谨其閒居之所为，非必此也，君子岂以耳目闻见为意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319249_comment'></div>即十目所视，十手所指，而有不睹不闻者多矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319249_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319249_comment'></div>此非执柯伐柯者之所能喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319249_comment'></div>吾虽欲自以为得耶，则兼山父子已先得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319249_comment'></div>吾言之而有合者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319249_comment'></div>彼其学于程氏，得于面命也，非诸生读语录比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319249_comment'></div>吾尝疑程录自有精意，如「鸢飞鱼跃」章语云：「与『必有事焉而勿正』之意相同，会得时活泼泼地，不会得只是弄精神」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319249_comment'></div>未必或者不以其禅也略之，非郭氏学于伊川，则必亦以为禅矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319249_comment'></div>虽然，非取节而言之，又表而出之，则子云复生，未可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319249_comment'></div>象山常疑《太极图》绝于吟风弄月之后，以此观之，又未必然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1319249_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='afa53bec24b84f0baa6ec659d1881102_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("afa53bec24b84f0baa6ec659d1881102");'><span id='afa53bec24b84f0baa6ec659d1881102_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年</a>，37岁</div><div id='afa53bec24b84f0baa6ec659d1881102' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年</a>　春夏闲居故乡庐陵。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b89f8d0914b34dd9923b05fa5e4274a6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b89f8d0914b34dd9923b05fa5e4274a6");'><span id='b89f8d0914b34dd9923b05fa5e4274a6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1273')">1269-1273年</a>，38-42岁</div><div id='b89f8d0914b34dd9923b05fa5e4274a6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年</a>　任中书架阁仅一月半，丁忧，罢归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年</a>　居家庐陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　儿子将孙在吉水文昌虎溪读书。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_91253'>五朝寿俊，算生平占得、淳熙四四。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91253'>三万六千三万了，剩有一千饶底。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91253'>三百年间，和风丽日，几个能销此。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91253'>约山山笑，先生不负山矣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91253_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91253'>今岁甲子重阳，待重数，五百十三甲子。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91253'>吟万首诗更自和，岁岁寿诗自喜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91253'>若比潞公，如今年纪，犹是平章事。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91253'>先生抚掌，问他闲日能几。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91253_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　居乡庐陵，有诗送李参政。作品：送李参政守庐陵归。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗今不存。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　居乡庐陵，时邓剡有词送李嘉廷守满，翁有词和。作品：《木兰花慢》（自崆峒麦熟）<div id='poem_90969' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_90969' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/90969?labeling=true' target='_blank'>木兰花慢<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>和中甫李参政席上韵</a><span id='poem_content_90969'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_90969'>自崆峒麦熟，耕犊满、桔槔闲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_90969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_90969'>笑吾党清谈，长衣櫑具，更进贤冠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_90969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_90969'>仓皇庇公宇下，便秋风、江上不惊寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_90969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_90969'>雪夜入三城易，槐阴护一家难。<div id='poem_sentence_3_90969_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_90969'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_90969", 90969, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>东山</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_90969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_90969'>零雨几时还。<div id='poem_sentence_5_90969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_90969'>领客竹林间。<div id='poem_sentence_6_90969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_90969'>看满座空尊，轻裘缓带，绿鬓朱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_90969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_90969'>风流一笑余事，定碑金、无恙庾家完。<div id='poem_sentence_8_90969_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_90969'>又赋南烹初食，明朝餐玉何山。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年</a>　居乡庐陵。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='31c8a72c62ef4d1b9cb776410a88f355_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("31c8a72c62ef4d1b9cb776410a88f355");'><span id='31c8a72c62ef4d1b9cb776410a88f355_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年</a>，44岁</div><div id='31c8a72c62ef4d1b9cb776410a88f355' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月</a>　居乡庐陵。闻贾似道督师兵败，有感作词。作品：《六州歌头》（向来人道）<div id='poem_90957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_90957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/90957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>六州歌头</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_90957")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_90957_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_90957'>乙亥二月，贾平章似道督师至太平州鲁港，未见敌，鸣锣而溃。后半月闻报，赋此</div><div id='poem_preface_90957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_90957'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_90957'>向来人道，真个胜周公。<div id='poem_sentence_0_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_90957'>燕然眇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_90957'>浯溪小。<div id='poem_sentence_2_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_90957'>万世功。<div id='poem_sentence_3_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_90957'>再建隆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_90957'>十五年宇宙，宫中膺。<div id='poem_sentence_5_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_90957'>堂中伴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_90957'>翻虎鼠，搏鹯雀，覆蛇龙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_90957'>鹤发庞眉，憔悴空山久，来上东封。<div id='poem_sentence_8_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_90957'>便一朝符瑞，四十万人同。<div id='poem_sentence_9_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_90957'>说甚东风。<div id='poem_sentence_10_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_90957'>怕西风。<div id='poem_sentence_11_90957_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_90957'>甚边尘起，渔阳惨。<div id='poem_sentence_12_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_90957'>霓裳断。<div id='poem_sentence_13_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_90957'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_90957", 90957, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>广寒宫</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_90957'>青楼杳。<div id='poem_sentence_15_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_90957'>朱门悄。<div id='poem_sentence_16_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_90957'>镜湖空。<div id='poem_sentence_17_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_90957'>里湖通。<div id='poem_sentence_18_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_90957'>大纛高牙去，人不见，港重重。<div id='poem_sentence_19_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_90957'>斜阳外，芳草碧，落花红。<div id='poem_sentence_20_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_90957'>抛尽黄金无计，方知道、前此和戎。<div id='poem_sentence_21_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_90957'>但千年传说，夜半一声铜。<div id='poem_sentence_22_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_90957'>何面江东。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_90957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年5月</a>　丞相陈宜中欲除为史馆检阅，请辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年10月</a>　本月除太学博士，因元兵逼近，断了江西前往临安的道路，未授。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='eca27a77dcc947aaa652212f752716cc_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　避祸永阳。有词。作品：《兰陵王》（送春去）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span>《青玉案》（无肠可断听花雨）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span><div id='poem_91004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91004?labeling=true' id='poem_content_91004'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91004'>送春去，春去人间无路。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91004'>秋千外，芳草连天，谁遣风沙暗南浦？<div id='poem_sentence_1_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91004'>依依甚意绪，漫忆海门飞絮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91004'>乱鸦过，斗转城荒，不见来时试灯处。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91004_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91004'>春去，最谁苦？<div id='poem_sentence_4_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91004'>但箭雁沉边，梁燕无主，杜鹃声里长门暮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91004'>想玉树凋土，泪盘如露。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91004'>咸阳送客屡回顾，斜日未能度。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91004_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91004'>春去，尚来否？<div id='poem_sentence_8_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91004'>正江令恨别，庾信愁赋，苏堤尽日风和雨。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91004'>叹神游故国，花记前度。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91004'>人生流落，顾孺子，共夜语。</div><div target='_blank'>青玉案<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>暮春旅怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_91090'>沈沈已是三更许。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91090'>如此残红那得住。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91090'>一春情绪，半生羁旅，寂寞空山语。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91090_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91090'>霖铃不是相思阻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91090'>四十平分犹过五。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　避祸永阳。本年秋，追和刘过多首《唐多令》词，有云：“丙子中秋前，闻歌此词者即席借芦叶满汀洲韵。”（明月满沧洲）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span>《唐多令》（寒雁下荒洲）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span>《唐多令》（风露小瀛洲洲）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span>《唐多令》（日落紫霞洲）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span><div id='poem_91128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91128' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91128")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_0_91128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91128'>长江一意流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91128'>除却月宫花树下，尘坱莽、欲何游。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91128_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐多令<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_5_91129'>灵胥还怒不。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91129'>满湖山、犹是春愁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91129'>欲向涌金门外去，烟共草、不堪游。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91129_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91127?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91127'>人间尘、不到琼楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91127'>错向五陵陵上望，几回月、几回秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91127_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91127'>落日太湖头。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91127'>垂虹今是不。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91127'>醉尊前、往往成愁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91127'>便有扁舟西子在，无汗漫、与君游。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91127_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91125?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91125'><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91125'>玉虹仙、如在黄楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91125'>何必锦袍吹玉笛，听欸乃、数声秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91125_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91125'>赤壁舞涛头。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91125'>周郎还到不。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91125'>倚西风、袅袅余愁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91125'>唤起横江飞道士，来伴我、月中游。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91125_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91132?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91132_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_sentence_0_91132'>零露下长洲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91132'>云翻海倒流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91132_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_91132_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91131' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91131' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91131?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91131'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91131'>残日下瓜洲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91131_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91131_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91131'>回首少年真可笑，无一事、又悲秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91131_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91131'>天在海边头。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91131_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91131'>天风有意不。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91131_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91131_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年8月15日</a>　避祸永阳。本年中秋节赏月，有填词。作品：《烛影摇红》（明月如冰）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span><div id='poem_91150' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91150' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91150?labeling=true' target='_blank'>烛影摇红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>丙子中秋泛月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91150")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91150_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91150'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91150'>明月如冰，乱云飞下斜河去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91150'>旋呼艇子载箫声，风景还如故。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91150'>袅袅余怀何许。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91150'>听尊前、呜呜似诉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91150'>近年潮信，万里阴晴，和天无据。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91150_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91150'>有客秋风，去时留下金盘露。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91150'>醉中休问，明月明年，人在何处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_91150_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　避祸永阳。儿子将孙二十岁生日，有词。作品：《临江仙》（二十年前此日）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span><div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年1月15日</a>　避祸永阳。有感于李清照《永遇乐》元夕词，追和一首，表达对故土的缅怀和伤痛。（璧月初晴）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span><div id='poem_91007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91007?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91007'>璧月初晴，黛云远澹，春事谁主。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91007'>禁苑<span class='link' id='poem_91136' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91136' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91136?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恋绣衾<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>宫中吹箫</a><span id='poem_sentence_3_91136'>天涯流落哀声在，听乌乌、不似内娇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91136'>漫身似、商人妇，泣孤舟、长夜寂寥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_91136_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　是年春，为乡友胡盘居生日作词。作品：《双调望江南》（盘之所）<div id='poem_91168' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91168' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91168?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆江南<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>胡盘居生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91168")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91168_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91168'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91168'>盘之所，春蝶舞晴暄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91168'>溪傍野梅根种玉，墙围脩竹笋生鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91168'>深院待回仙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91168_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91168'>嘉熙好，四十二年前。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91168'>犹记五星丁卯聚，更迟几岁甲申连。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91168'>快活共千年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_91168_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年9月14日</a>　本年九月友人周溪园（应合）生日，辰翁有寿词。作品：《水调歌头》（先生岂我辈）<span class='inlineComment2'>（年份据吴熊和等《唐宋词汇评·两宋卷》第3770页。）</span>《水调歌头》（似似不常似）<div id='poem_90997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_90997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/90997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>寿周溪园，有序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年9月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_90997")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_90997_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_90997'>天九积阳，月半将望。恭惟某官，嘉定间气，西江耆英。乔木南山，为人父，为众父；光风霁月，有一天，有二天。固宜十万户之民，同致八千秋之祝。某俚歌水调，上赞金丹，辄陈宗工，窃幸微眄。</div><div id='poem_preface_90997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_90997'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_90997'>先生岂我辈，造物乃其徒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_90997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_90997'>荷衣自放林壑，亦未弃银鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_90997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_90997'>留得东篱晚节，笑倒龙山秃帽，一醉插茱萸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_90997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_90997'>天下有大老，携手盍归乎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_90997_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_90997'>别头经，三昼梦，一编书。<div id='poem_sentence_4_90997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_90997'>向之麟者止矣，且看老溪图。<div id='poem_sentence_5_90997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_90997'>历遍后天既未，依约明朝三五，乾体适当符。<div id='poem_sentence_6_90997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_90997'>还以奉公寿，不是讲鹅湖。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_90997_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年9月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91000")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91000_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_91000'>日献洞宾公像于溪园先生，报以阶庭府公耐轩寿容，曰：是类吾子。且三叠前水调以证之，于是某得自号为小耐矣。虽甚无似，不敢当。顾公所览揆如此，谊不虚辱，敢续之好歌，毋忘佳话。</div><div id='poem_preface_91000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91000'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91000'>似似不常似，似我一生徒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91000'>画工自画龙种，忽近海飞鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91000'>大笑北宫称弟，遂使西河疑女，同气自椒萸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91000'>且谓杜公者，即是老君乎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91000_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91000'>日给华，芎藭本，薛羊书。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91000'>马师真只这是，可是躄浮图。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91000'>大小卢同马异，天下使君与操，但欠虎铜符。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91000_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91000'>说甚左眼痣，已过洞庭湖。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91000_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　本年还为朱佐撰写书楼记。作品：《古山楼记》<div id='poem_1319376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>古山楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319376")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319376'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319376'>长沙朱君佐过予于庐陵，相视各壮岁也，已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319376_comment'></div>年近五十，书来语我，古青之楼将栖隐焉，求文以为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319376_comment'></div>余为记之曰：青者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319376_comment'></div>山也，请更之古山如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319376_comment'></div>山在天地间几千万年而未化，如骈枝疣赘而莫之胜说，岂惟人病是，将阴阳者厌之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319376_comment'></div>吾亦不知其初，高下磊落，变化何以至此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319376_comment'></div>以为大块之所壅，而洪水之所决邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319376_comment'></div>其高且数百千丈，为日月相避隐处，殆造物之所不能去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319376_comment'></div>意者其亦有杞国之故，且坠且积，以及此邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319376_comment'></div>求之六合之内而不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319376_comment'></div>虽神州赤县吾不信也，异乎此者其当何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319376_comment'></div>何厚何高？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319376_comment'></div>何颉何颃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319376_comment'></div>于是有共工者触之，于是有五丁者凿之，于是有愚公者移之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319376_comment'></div>触之、凿之、移之之不可，则鞭之以秦皇，拔之以项羽，蹴之以夸父而不胜，而衡守，而擅铸，而媚之以封禅，而阨之以兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319376_comment'></div>其穷人力若此，而谓天地欲无意焉不可也，谓天地有意乎后之人益不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319376_comment'></div>而后之人若有力焉，方其自恃也，有过此焉，而卒不可恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319376_comment'></div>彼其有助于人也亦多矣，其助之不可而因以敝之，与其敝者自敝，而独与天地者相终始也，悲哉乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319376_comment'></div>所谓古山者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319376_comment'></div>吾与君登楼而望君所居岳麓，循岳而南，为苍梧之野，二妃之所霣泪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319376_comment'></div>南至于罗浮，望三山者或彷佛焉，今其人远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319376_comment'></div>少西为洞庭，又西为峨眉之雪，蚕丛、鱼凫者不可得而道已，每闻子规，喟然而起，起而望，曰望帝，今其人远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319376_comment'></div>自江入于海，则东也其山曰涂山，玉帛万国，专车藏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319376_comment'></div>又东为沧海，安期、徐生自是而不返，今其人远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319376_comment'></div>言未既，君振袖而起曰：「荒哉万古，阔乎其四方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319376_comment'></div>吾楼于是间也何居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319376_comment'></div>其旷然若古今之涂乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319376_comment'></div>其亦他有所可隐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319376_comment'></div>子盍为我言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319376_comment'></div>子不为我言之，旷也奈何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319376_comment'></div>余仰而噫，俯而笑曰：今犹古也，今之古者其犹有存乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319376_comment'></div>则余不得与于斯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319376_comment'></div>子又以今之今者为足存乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319376_comment'></div>夜以思之，其知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319376_comment'></div>其自明日以往，抑不可知，余以斯楼为不足乐邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319376_comment'></div>四方若此，君楼居而我记之，其复何憾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319376_comment'></div>井干丽谯，临春结绮，盛时钜丽者安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319376_comment'></div>下至齐云、丰乐、岳阳、黄鹤，骚人畴昔徘徊落日，又焉知其至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319376_comment'></div>则夫斯楼者其不足记邪，其不谓之隐耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319376_comment'></div>夫四方而不足以为隐，则隐此足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319376_comment'></div>隐而谓吾山，则吾山矣，山在天地间谁能主之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319376_comment'></div>四岳三涂，是不一姓，以吾隐此，而山亦吾，则山与君俱不可得而见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319376_comment'></div>不能不在人间而藏于人间，异时欲知君者求之楼，欲知君楼者求之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319376_comment'></div>记成于己卯庚辰之春日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319376_comment'></div>是日也，雾漫天，自子规、南二妃、西青青者如失，惟朱氏楼独存。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1319376_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='261d5155647d49b8942468b2dc8ca30d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("261d5155647d49b8942468b2dc8ca30d");'><span id='261d5155647d49b8942468b2dc8ca30d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>，48岁</div><div id='261d5155647d49b8942468b2dc8ca30d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　应白鹭洲书院山长之请，作纪念江万里文。作品：《鹭洲书院江文忠公祠堂记》<div id='poem_1319340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹭洲书院江文忠公祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319340")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319340'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319340'>故大丞相、赠太师、益国江文忠公古心先生祠鹭洲，侑欧公，己卯曹山长奇所作也，于是谥文忠四三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319340_comment'></div>厩廪荒凉，矧暇俎豆，至曹君始有意教事，以及乎此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319340_comment'></div>祠成，闻者垂涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319340_comment'></div>先生生庆元戊午，遭伪禁之世，父师窃窃传习朱氏，处白鹿，游东湖，所交多考亭门人，出入端平诸老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319340_comment'></div>其为吾州，年四十有三，声名德业，高迈前闻，故能创鹭洲如白鹿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319340_comment'></div>深衣入林，媚映前后，无不心醉名理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319340_comment'></div>然所聘不过十数名士，而缙绅德之，吏民怜之，悍卒化之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319340_comment'></div>去之四十年，贤侯健吏其何不有，同时父老化为异物，而识与不识曰古心古心如昨，曰江检详者亦如作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319340_comment'></div>岂惟吾州士论胜而民俗厚，亦先生之流风系人心，能使其没世不忘如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319340_comment'></div>盖尝痛名贤之在天地间如风雨，其变化及物，关系晦明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319340_comment'></div>极其所至，曾何足以当俄顷之运，而鼓之动之，沛然如出乎六合之外者声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319340_comment'></div>虽复身数朝家，累世寿考，且百年之久，而又能不殄厥愠，不陨厥问，以有成也，要亦如风雨过之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319340_comment'></div>而谗者败之，忌者离之，不肖者塞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319340_comment'></div>当先生之盛年，则有不见释于乡人者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319340_comment'></div>藉第令其人亡恙，亦谁复比数，而先生之所存每抑而愈彰，已远而弥长者声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319340_comment'></div>计其三四起家，直出于谗者之疏，忌者之远，不肖者之隙，复何能遂其志，行其道，展其四体，而闻其名者愿其有所成，谅其犹有馀蕴，虽善不足以相及，而犹欣然乐之者声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319340_comment'></div>凡大人之行，其声宜如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319340_comment'></div>先生閒居，其志念在国家，其精神在庐陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319340_comment'></div>往从班时，尝问叶西涧庐陵曾得士否，因为言布衣数士环堵水竹间意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319340_comment'></div>西涧退而叹曰：「吾至庐陵梦耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319340_comment'></div>咸淳初，发德音欲求诸儒之后，时宰以先生自建来，主朱氏，先生奏曰：「臣在建安，收奖朱氏备至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319340_comment'></div>今世所少惟节义，有以死易节，而子孙仅得一泽，后遂不振绝望者，以臣所知，近年庐陵胡梦昱可念也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319340_comment'></div>繇是廷评后得擢用，又议谥廷评忠公，不果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319340_comment'></div>其用意类尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319340_comment'></div>即增贡额，减岁籴，荐进除目，或用或不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319340_comment'></div>常事无足论，乃其经世则有大愿矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319340_comment'></div>再相再不合，尝叹平生志气之乐，惟鹭洲一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319340_comment'></div>过江百年，仁山字水，人自为士，然学校科举终有愧于道，孰能学校科举外而求志，又孰能因学校科举而成之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319340_comment'></div>自鹭洲兴，而后斯人宿于义理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319340_comment'></div>自鹭洲兴，而后言义理者畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319340_comment'></div>又不惟文字而已，而后学者知矫其质习，存其气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319340_comment'></div>又不惟气象而已，而后立身名节，一以先生台谏为风采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319340_comment'></div>推论人才长育之自，斯文一变而至欧公，再变而至先生，而先生又以身徇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319340_comment'></div>宇宙与之终始，虽康之山、番之水同光而共洁，而其道隐然增鹭洲之重，与欧公而并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319340_comment'></div>其好士似欧公，论谏似欧公，变文体似欧公，而又得谥似欧公，受乡人毁似欧公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319340_comment'></div>欧公老颍，而先生祀吉，老颍者有所避，而祀吉者以其思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319340_comment'></div>呜呼，岂偶然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319340_comment'></div>方其为鹭洲，四方书院未有萌，其后遍，诸贤论建实始此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319340_comment'></div>顾独尝有遗恨，欲修鹭洲，仆前碑为续记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319340_comment'></div>虽未能知其何意，然昔者吾见其《考亭书院记》矣，曰如以名而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319340_comment'></div>穷山空谷，袂属肩随，人以为此学之盛，而由更事者旁观而窃叹，乃不如昔者退学于伪禁之时，信之之深而得之之实也，则吾亦为世道隐之于心久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319340_comment'></div>然则续记虽不作可知也，意者其在斯乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319340_comment'></div>某事先生十有五年，日所见之犹史，独为庐陵言则言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319340_comment'></div>先生玉立如山，和气在眉睫间如柳，声含弘如量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319340_comment'></div>登斯堂，望二公者，不知山川之气何时而复生，而又安知其不共天风而下也？</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1319340_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='20cd6c4de7ed4d52a36f22a88bf39c3c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("20cd6c4de7ed4d52a36f22a88bf39c3c");'><span id='20cd6c4de7ed4d52a36f22a88bf39c3c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>，49岁</div><div id='20cd6c4de7ed4d52a36f22a88bf39c3c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>　从彭泽返回庐陵，鄱阳柴景实来访。作序相送。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='efb254cb24ca41da8b47c9beb39134dc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("efb254cb24ca41da8b47c9beb39134dc");'><span id='efb254cb24ca41da8b47c9beb39134dc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>，49岁</div><div id='efb254cb24ca41da8b47c9beb39134dc' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>居乡庐陵。作品：《减字木兰花》（送春待晓）<div id='poem_91164' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91164' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91164?labeling=true' target='_blank'>减字木兰花<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>庚辰送春</a><span class='authorDate'>（1280年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91164")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91164_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91164'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91164'>送春待晓。春是五更先去了。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91164'>我醉方知。春正怜伊怕别伊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91164_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91164'>留君不可。归到海边方忆我。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91164'>做尽花归。欲赠君时少一枝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91164'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_91164_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>茶陵陈俊来访，辰翁作记送之。作品：《汲古堂记》<div id='poem_1319344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汲古堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1280年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319344")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319344'>汲古堂者，宋公子诸生国学之堂名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319344_comment'></div>尝有井，故云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319344_comment'></div>德祐鼎迁，堂废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319344_comment'></div>又七年，学燬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319344_comment'></div>而铅山前释褐进士赵嗣德以其重修大义桥之寺、之井、之堂，亦名之曰汲古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319344_comment'></div>汲古者又过江初邯郸贾逸祖所自号也，先生则嗣德之祖之友，南来依于赵于寺，学焉赋焉，死而葬焉，章泉赵蕃表之曰「宋诗人贾元放」者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319344_comment'></div>至是祖而配焉，又取诸章泉配焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319344_comment'></div>登斯堂，酌斯泉者，低徊乔木之下，如过周墟，观鲁庙，无不仰止其名而怜伤其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319344_comment'></div>复求文于余以记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319344_comment'></div>余为之长太息曰：莫古于天，天者不平之积也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319344_comment'></div>由今言之，亦孰非古也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319344_comment'></div>第论前日峨峨堂下，安知其至此，其至此无怪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319344_comment'></div>南渡百年，奸臣擅者五六，久矣夫，福威之不惟辟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319344_comment'></div>姑为君宗衮而言之，毁金縢，被霜露，閒居闻问之党遍天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319344_comment'></div>当其时，非圣主意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319344_comment'></div>凡咈天理，负人事，宁独此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319344_comment'></div>其平世所谓敌国者，直弹击文致口语而已，流恣于近年，班朝绿野，愚寡冲如，黔首冤怒激极，震电横彗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319344_comment'></div>诞取前史所谓宦官、外戚、藩镇、权臣，以为是反复迭起不可解之宇宙者，一反手而胜无遗，而古有不足为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319344_comment'></div>吾尝叹夫日所见之犹史，或言与事悖，事与情异，颇疑文字以来欺世也皆若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319344_comment'></div>其为苍苍冥冥者忿而欲塞，务使能言之类亦如其不能言，而古有不足信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319344_comment'></div>今子之读书是堂也，其能得夫世外者而志之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319344_comment'></div>其亦不免于传闻所传闻也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319344_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319344_comment'></div>子亦知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319344_comment'></div>古之所存者今不必有，今之所有又古之所无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319344_comment'></div>古犹汲也，其陈乎吾前者或废或绝，则或地下者有之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319344_comment'></div>故冢之书，泗之鼎，岘山之石，参差零落，出于千载陵谷之有待，然而汲者希矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319344_comment'></div>古犹汲也，必竭而后新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319344_comment'></div>今吾雷同诸老之后，常一经而百传，复欲舍是而图之，则必僭先贤而背师说，虽童子亦且以为不可，然而汲者新矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319344_comment'></div>直心盛年高尚，甫得一第，即唾弃归而养志，此其中有大过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319344_comment'></div>斯堂何许，宛其麟止，傥能得夫元放、章泉之为友，揽古所谓不平之恨，肆而评之，当有出于众人之所不讲，是为汲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319344_comment'></div>恨吾不能赞其志，徒想见斯泉于重湖之上，万山之外，寓焉言之，发其微而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319344_comment'></div>抑惠山如海，发于梦寐，有寺僧者谬之曰在是，则在是矣，是得之华池者犹惠山也，亦所谓汲也，则吾与子得不已相见于此堂与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319344_comment'></div>直心，德字也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319344_comment'></div>友元放者，其曾祖赠金紫彦孟也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319344_comment'></div>友章泉者，祖龙图充夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319344_comment'></div>桥县北，寺桥北，桥寺一新，桥最钜<span class='inlineComment2'>（《须溪集》卷三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319344_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1319344'>德字也：疑当作「嗣德字也」，即上文赵嗣德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1319344_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='352899ef57c9425c9991c7ccadd9104f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("352899ef57c9425c9991c7ccadd9104f");'><span id='352899ef57c9425c9991c7ccadd9104f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1283')">1281-1283年</a>，50-52岁</div><div id='352899ef57c9425c9991c7ccadd9104f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年5月5日</a>　本年端午节，辰翁在回乡途中过，有追和陈简斋词。作品：《临江仙》（旧日采莲羞半面）<div id='poem_91105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91105?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十三 </span>辛巳端午和陈简斋韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91105")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91105'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91105'>旧日采莲羞半面，至今回首匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91105'>梦穿斜日水云红。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91105'>痴心犹独自，等待郑公风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91105_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91105'>海上颓云潮不返，侧身空堕辽东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91105'>人间天上几时同。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91105'>宫衣元不遇，无语醉醒中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_91105_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年8月10日</a>　本年闰八月，辰翁自黄州归乡，有词序云：“辛巳前八月九日夜，自黄州步归，……明日为赋此寄之。”作品：《水调歌头》（山水无宿约）<div id='poem_90984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_90984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/90984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年8月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_90984")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_90984_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_90984'>辛巳前八月九日夜，自黄州步归，萧英甫以舟泛余舣本觉寺门外，夜深未能睡，明日为赋此寄之。</div><div id='poem_preface_90984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_90984'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_90984'>山水无宿约，村暗自当还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_90984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_90984'>不知有客乘兴，载我弄沧湾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_90984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_90984'>酒吸明河欲尽，月落三星在下，未放水风闲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_90984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_90984'>影转松起舞，扶步入林间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_90984_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_90984'>恨无人，横野笛，叫关山。<div id='poem_sentence_4_90984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_90984'>知君慷慨何事，惜得米阳关。<div id='poem_sentence_5_90984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_90984'>看取大江东去，把酒凄然北望，说著泪潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_90984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_90984'>我饮自须尽，君唱有何难。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_90984_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年9月9日</a>　本年重阳节，辰翁和乡友刘仲简有唱和词，序云：“和刘仲简九日韵。”作品：《沁园春》（九日黄花）<div id='poem_52298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_52298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/52298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>和刘仲简九日韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_52298")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_52298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_52298'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_52298'>九日黄花，渊明之后，谁当汝俦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_52298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_52298'>记龙山昨夜，寒泉九井，帽轻似叶，须戟如虬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_52298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_52298'>庚扇西风，孔林落照，银海横波十二楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_52298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_52298'>闲笑道，那华亭上蔡，再见何由。<div id='poem_sentence_3_52298_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_52298'>人生似我何求。<div id='poem_sentence_4_52298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_52298'>算惟有高人高处游。<div id='poem_sentence_5_52298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_52298'>笑如今别驾，前时方外，尘埃半百，岁月如流。<div id='poem_sentence_6_52298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_52298'>如此连墙，今年不见，一首犹胜万户侯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_52298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_52298'>偷闲好，便明朝有约，莫莫休休。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_52298_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年</a>　居乡庐陵，以诗文会友。作品：《摸鱼儿》（道醉乡、无边无岸）<div id='poem_91213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91213")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91213_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91213'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91213'>三百年、人间天上，遽如许、遽如许。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91213'>落花寒食东风雨，漠漠长陵抔土。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91213'>魂归否。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91213'>怕些不分明，又堕人笺疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91213'>且无相负。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91213'>记昔与诸贤，共谈洛下，曾识老人父。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91213_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91213'>牛衣泪，冷落闻鸡东府。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91213'>风尘曾独深虑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91213'>子规声断长门晓，春梦不堪重做。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91213'>千万古。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91213'>但目极心伤，宛转虞兮楚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91213'>江东日暮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91213'>想野草荒田，而今何处，不待雍门鼓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91213_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91212' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91212' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91212?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91212_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_91212'>今岁海棠迟开半月，然一夕如雪，无饮余者，赋此寄恨。</div><div id='poem_preface_91212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91212'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91212'>是他家、绛唇翠袖，可容卿有功否。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91212'>相思不到胭脂井，只隔东林烟柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91212'>春去又。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91212'>漫一夜东风，吹得花成旧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91212'>无人举酒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91212'>但照影堤流，图他红泪，飘洒到襟袖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91212_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91212'>人间事，大半归谋诸妇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91212'>不如意十八九。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91212'>敲门夜半窥园李，赤脚玉川惊走。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91212'>何处有。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91212'>更炙烛风流，看到人归后。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91212'>休休回首。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91212'>笑旧日园林，佺巢蜀锦，处处可携手。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91212_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91216?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91216_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91216'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91216'>正何须、阳关肠断，吴姬苦劝人酒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91216'>中年怀抱萦萦处，看取伴烟和柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91216'>柳摇首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91216'>笑飞到家山，已是酴醾后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91216'>留连话旧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91216'>问溪上儿童，颇曾见我，有此故人否。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91216_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91216'>相逢地，还忆今宵三韭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91216'>青山知了迎候。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91216'>东风自送归帆去，吹得乱红沾袖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91216'>暮云皱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91216'>听杜宇高高，啼向无何有。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91216'>江花垂手。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91216'>任春色重来，江花更好，难可少年又。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91216_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91215?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91215'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91215'>待欲归、家山未得，方知名不如酒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91215'>丹砂便做金勾漏，难遣鬓青似柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91215'>试搔首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91215'>记移竹南塘，又是三年后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91215'>情怀非旧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91215'>叹少日相如，垆边老去，能赋上林否。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91215_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91215'>种兰处，赢得青青种韭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91215'>渊明中路相候。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91215'>何须更待三三径，也自长拖衫袖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91215'>青袍皱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91215'>便持当金貂，赊取邻家有。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91215'>小儿拍手。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91215'>笑昨醉如泥，盟言止酒，何事醒来又。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91215_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91208?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91208'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91208'>醉与君、狂歌又笑，不知当日何调。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91208'>孤山梅下吟魂冷，说甚那时苏小。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91208'>沧波眇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91208'>奈此岛，累累竟是谁家表。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91208'>归欤白鸟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91208'>看四圣飘香，朱门金榜，化作竺飞峤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91208_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91208'>衰也久，旧游梦翠禽绕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91208'>坱兮轧、皎兮窈。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91208'>相思一夜窗前白，谁识余怀渺渺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91208'>残年了。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91208'>听画角，悲凉又是霜天晓。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91208'>馀音杳缈。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91208'>叹五十之年，我加八九，君隔几科诏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91208_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年</a>　本年冬，与邓剡多有唱和。有和梅词等。作品：《摸鱼儿》（记歌头辛壬癸甲）<div id='poem_91207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91207?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>辛巳冬和中斋梅词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91207")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91207'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91207'>记歌头、辛壬癸甲，乌乌能知谁晓。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91207'>梅花不待元宵好，雪月交光独照。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91207'>愁未老。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91207'>更老似渠鬓，冷面迎相笑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91207'>君词定峭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91207'>但减十年前，偎桃傍李，肯独为梅好。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91207_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91207'>山中好。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91207'>可但一枝春早。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91207'>道边无限花草。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91207'>米嘉荣共何戡在，还忆永新娇小。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91207'>明年了。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91207'>又唤起流莺，又自愁鹃叫。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91207'>东皇太昊。<div id='poem_sentence_12_91207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_91207'>更不是琼花，香无半点，一笑使人倒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_91207_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年12月24日</a>　本年生日，有自寿词。作品：《摸鱼儿》（是耶非吾年如此）<div id='poem_91203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91203?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十九 </span>辛巳自寿年五十</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年12月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91203")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91203_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91203'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91203'>是耶非、吾年如此，更痴更悔今昨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91203'>狂吟近日疏于酒，转似秋山瘦削。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91203'>浑未觉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91203'>恁儿子门生，前度登高弱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91203'>情怀又恶。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91203'>叹亲友中年，不堪离别，况复久零落。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91203_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91203'>长生药。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91203'>有分神仙难学。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91203'>人生聊复行乐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91203'>百年半梦随流水，半在南枝北萼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91203'>妾命薄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91203'>但寂寞黄昏，时听城楼角。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91203'>愁无可著。<div id='poem_sentence_12_91203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_91203'>且取醉尊前，明朝休问，昨日已忘却。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_91203_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年12月30日</a>　本年除夕，辰翁不胜感慨，有词。作品：《捉拍丑奴儿》（送岁可无诗）<div id='poem_91106' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91106' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91106?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摊破南乡子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>辛巳除夕</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年12月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91106")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91106_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91106'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91106'>送岁可无诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91106'>得团栾、忍不开眉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91106'>不记去年今夕梦，江东怀抱，江西信息，舍北妻儿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91106_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91106'>五十扊扅炊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91106'>待五十、富贵成痴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91106'>百年苦乐乘除看，今年一半，明年一半，更似儿时。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_91106_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年</a>　庐陵同乡刘自昭为其芷堂求记。作品：《芷堂记》<div id='poem_1319384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319384?labeling=true' target='_blank'>芷堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319384")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319384_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319384'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319384'>吾同姓自昭居何山，近市如陋巷，家惟芷一本，五十年根浮瓮，香出屋，客至意销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319384_comment'></div>有羡焉欲得之者，其家尊曰：「吾父所植也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319384_comment'></div>问自昭，曰：「吾祖所植也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319384_comment'></div>无不恻然已，惘然去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319384_comment'></div>比年马之过市也如织，高垣重闭，丹青草木无得保所素玩，矧是美植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319384_comment'></div>然睨者不至，至者不取，亦若有守之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319384_comment'></div>问何道，自昭曰：「吾惟托之无可奈何，而亦无与竞也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319384_comment'></div>问其所以培壅而寿，自昭曰：「自吾见吾父未尝溉，溉亦无所受，根而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319384_comment'></div>片篷芘日，雪霜亦于是，其得于天者狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319384_comment'></div>今其叶可二尺，而花之层出者拔其萃以长，比他植最早，又后衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319384_comment'></div>吾与之生长，更世大变，以及乎此，愿有以记之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319384_comment'></div>盖自何山百里求予记于荒林之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319384_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319384_comment'></div>吾城居人也，往年辟一室号「问不知」，有方外道人养盆芷廿年，舁以好我，岁再花而予迁，迁而避于方山之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319384_comment'></div>它日过吾居，未焚，有马于庭方龁是根以饱，予闵然三叹，赋之去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319384_comment'></div>彼其芳也与予同，又养于方外不为浅，然一入吾室，曾不能芘其足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319384_comment'></div>今君之穷也三世而芳如昨，虽眷焉爱之，而不溉不修，自然而已，不迁不吝，亦自然而已，此其有数存乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319384_comment'></div>意者亦君之祖德有以阴种之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319384_comment'></div>昔之知数者于一花、一叶、一饮食而占其盛衰，况大寒大暑，大兵大乱，三世五十年之久，无所芘赖，无敢爱，无敢害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319384_comment'></div>王之槐，魏之紫，方、陈之荔，或更代易姓，为人所感叹，而君之芷亦异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319384_comment'></div>诗书容膝，子孙绕前，花时对客，墙沽老瓦，近而抚之目睫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319384_comment'></div>旧庐旧邑，不见乔木，此何生在上而芬犹未沬，兢兢焉不出户庭，若得于天者，侥倖至足，此其足恃以久也，而岂独此芷之为验哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319384_comment'></div>予于是愧君矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319384_comment'></div>虽然，有患是花也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319384_comment'></div>五十年藏于市如隐，今君之号芷堂也始著，则后之求君者必于芷，求芷者必于君，君得无累是芷乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319384_comment'></div>夫予之芷已若芷矣，又为君记之，虽君不累，得无予累之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319384_comment'></div>君曰：「吾惟惧兹芳之易朽，以及此也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319384_comment'></div>则为约曰：吾为君记耳，藏于君，藏于君子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319384_comment'></div>君之芷五十年矣，又五十年乃出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319384_comment'></div>先五十年为绍定壬辰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1319384_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年5月5日</a>　本年端午，辰翁有感填词金缕曲一首，题曰“壬午五日”。作品：《金缕曲》（叶叶跳珠雨）<div id='poem_91081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91081' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_11_91081_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年7月7日</a>　本年七夕节，辰翁有感填词临江仙一首，题曰“壬午七夕”。作品：《临江仙》（天际何分南与北）<div id='poem_91093' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91093' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年8月15日</a>　本年中秋节天雨不见月，辰翁有感填词虞美人一首，题曰“壬午中秋雨后不见月”。作品：《虞美人》（湿云待向三更吐）<div id='poem_91232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91232' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年10月1日</a>　十月初一，为宋代冬季暖炉日，辰翁有词，题曰：“壬午开炉日戏作”作品：《汉宫春》（雨入轻寒）<div id='poem_91009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91009' class='poemTitle id='poem_title_91009_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91009'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91009'>雨入轻寒，但新篘未试，荒了东篱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91009'>朝来暗惊翠袖，重倚屏帏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91009'>明窗丽阁，为何人、冷落多时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91009'>催重顿，妆台侧畔，画堂未怕春迟。<div class='label1' id='c0ade7813cc44ac1803b2d78fd6a7d56_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c0ade7813cc44ac1803b2d78fd6a7d56");'><span id='c0ade7813cc44ac1803b2d78fd6a7d56_link'
