href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年9月</a>　为庐陵县治习溪桥作记。作品：《习溪桥记》<div id='poem_1319380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>习溪桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1283年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319380")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319380'>吾州习溪桥，永新下阳汤信叔为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319380_comment'></div>初，咸淳癸酉夏，水甚桥圮，三铁牛见，识曰赤乌二年，或曰桥是年五月廿四造牛云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319380_comment'></div>水去，民病涉，予谓太守黄同年镛曰：「市桥腰也，昼夜杂沓，何啻十数万人，褰裳缘木，负担提携，自坠攀高，车覆蹄颠，岂三十六万石为郡而不能复一桥」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319380_comment'></div>器之曰：「吾日补前政数十缗折欠且不足，安取此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319380_comment'></div>子其以美言出众力大成之，郡为倡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319380_comment'></div>予曰：「诺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319380_comment'></div>桥疏成，久之，会吏赃没数十万，余谓郡僚曰：「此独不可桥乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319380_comment'></div>亟入白，许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319380_comment'></div>久之桥成，又久之桥屋成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319380_comment'></div>其难如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319380_comment'></div>繇癸酉至壬午十年耳，乃五月廿四日最大水高，戊辰水又数尺，繇南栅门边长涝之屋漂者如市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319380_comment'></div>枝牵牛决，抵桥桥坏，桥数栋为前驱，虽址幸无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319380_comment'></div>稽其日与铁牛合，殆何数也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319380_comment'></div>既数月，海舟急，工役沸兴，山林贯输桥，僧以此时丐桥柱汤氏，汤顾之曰：「吾以羁旅，脱盗难苟，造舟有馀者无不施」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319380_comment'></div>或曰施寓言耳，然不逾月桥成，成而壮于旧倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319380_comment'></div>图经云：槠木桥，唐天宝七年县令吴励置，不知何年改习溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319380_comment'></div>习溪为城南甫六百年，自有此溪则有桥，而谓天宝始，则吴令之云也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319380_comment'></div>意者亦必有记也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319380_comment'></div>天壤以来，为吴令者多矣，而相望于无闻，无记故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319380_comment'></div>微咸淳铁牛见，则孰知此桥自吴赤乌造哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319380_comment'></div>此赤乌牛耳，桥不始此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319380_comment'></div>以蜀三犀證之，则桥亦始此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319380_comment'></div>是三牺却水患，济行役，不为县则为市，于今亦六千二百六十四甲子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319380_comment'></div>赣江南来，每春雨积，夏雪翻，湖拥西江涨，江壅习溪涨，涨未有不冒桥退，岁或再至三至，不再三至者亦无虑不浩荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319380_comment'></div>阅千数百水，而桥始一坏，赤乌始一见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319380_comment'></div>何古之作者如此其厚且固也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319380_comment'></div>而作者亦无闻焉，又何厚也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319380_comment'></div>桥于地用龙行，以吾所见，如吴之垂虹，闽之水西，泉之洛阳，不论扬州、金陵、钱塘、姑苏，又略彴小者亦不可为数，无不葱青阑干，雕丽蜿蜒，垂杨过雨，鞍马如画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319380_comment'></div>是桥朴陋，不当一沟一曲，而成之难，则郡之坏也久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319380_comment'></div>以其坏之久，成之难，而汤氏以一言之信，一人之力，一月之久，间海舟之役，俛焉为之而人不知，此吾所以记也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319380_comment'></div>虽然，自吾小年见是桥盛时为社林、州祠，为官药肆、为旗亭，歌钟列妓，长街灯火，饮者争席，定场设贾，呵道而后能过，往往可厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319380_comment'></div>然咸淳新造而旗亭废矣，十年再过而灯火稀、车盖息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319380_comment'></div>今其栋宇高坚，江山呈露，声销尘歇，未必不胜旧时，而市井老人，行歌还顾，自不能无所感也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319380_comment'></div>于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319380_comment'></div>鹭洲横陈，石梁县瀑，亦有孺子萧然而濯足者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319380_comment'></div>为我候之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319380_comment'></div>信叔复买地桥西，又屋以栖守僧，又将买田作僧供供佛，皆不可以不记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319380_comment'></div>桥成壬午十有二月，明年九月郡人刘某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1319380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年12月</a>　为庐陵乡贤王槐城寿，有词三首。序云：“槐城赋以自寿，又和韵见寿，三和谢之”作品：《念奴娇》（先生自寿）《念奴娇》（枯寒生晚）《念奴娇》（吾年如此）<div id='poem_91051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>槐城赋以自寿，又和韵见寿，三和谢之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1283年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91051")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91051'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91051'>先生自寿，拥衾寒，重赋凌云游意。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91051'>我有大儿孔文举，弱冠骎骎暮齿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91051'>桃已三偷，树犹如此，前度花开几。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91051'>蓬莱可塞，还童却老无计。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91051_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91051'>为此援笔翩翩，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_91051", 91051, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>大江东去</span>，好似歌头起。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91051'>寄与两家孙又子，长看以文为戏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91051'>某所某公，同年同月，谁剪招魂纸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91051'>前三例好，不须举后三例。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91051_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1283年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91053")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91053'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91053'>枯寒生晚，复何似、张绪少年时意。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91053'>薄命不逢何至此，满眼啼妆龋齿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91053'>城是城非，年来年去，万八千能几。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91053'>半痴半了，更痴儿计孙计。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91053_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91053'>回首仕已半生，仕何如已，已矣羞拈起。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91053'>幸有橘丸丸日大，且复从公围戏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91053'>若论弹文，更书谤箧，吾历无馀纸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91053'>多年致仕，大都有甚恩例。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91053_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91052?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1283年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91052'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91052'>吾年如此，更梦里、犹作狼居胥意。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91052'>千首新诗千斛酒，管甚何侯侯齿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91052'>员峤波翻，瀛洲尘败，吾屐能销几。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91052'>经丘寻壑，是他早计迟计。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91052_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91052'>犹记辰巳嗟嗟，故人贺我，且勉呼君起。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91052'>五十不来来过二，方悟人言都戏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91052'>以我情怀，借公篇韵，恨不天为纸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91052'>馀生一笑，不须邴曼容例。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91052_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年12月30日</a>　本年守岁，有词。作品：《摸鱼儿》（是疑他、春来倏忽）<div id='poem_91213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91213")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91213_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91213'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91213'>三百年、人间天上，遽如许、遽如许。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91213'>落花寒食东风雨，漠漠长陵抔土。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91213'>魂归否。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91213'>怕些不分明，又堕人笺疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91213'>且无相负。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91213'>记昔与诸贤，共谈洛下，曾识老人父。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91213_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91213'>牛衣泪，冷落闻鸡东府。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91213'>风尘曾独深虑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91213'>子规声断长门晓，春梦不堪重做。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91213'>千万古。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91213'>但目极心伤，宛转虞兮楚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91213'>江东日暮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91213'>想野草荒田，而今何处，不待雍门鼓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91213_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91212' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91212' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91212?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91212_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_91212'>今岁海棠迟开半月，然一夕如雪，无饮余者，赋此寄恨。</div><div id='poem_preface_91212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91212'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91212'>是他家、绛唇翠袖，可容卿有功否。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91212'>相思不到胭脂井，只隔东林烟柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91212'>春去又。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91212'>漫一夜东风，吹得花成旧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91212'>无人举酒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91212'>但照影堤流，图他红泪，飘洒到襟袖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91212_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91212'>人间事，大半归谋诸妇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91212'>不如意十八九。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91212'>敲门夜半窥园李，赤脚玉川惊走。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91212'>何处有。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91212'>更炙烛风流，看到人归后。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91212'>休休回首。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91212'>笑旧日园林，佺巢蜀锦，处处可携手。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91212_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91216?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91216_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91216'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91216'>正何须、阳关肠断，吴姬苦劝人酒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91216'>中年怀抱萦萦处，看取伴烟和柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91216'>柳摇首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91216'>笑飞到家山，已是酴醾后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91216'>留连话旧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91216'>问溪上儿童，颇曾见我，有此故人否。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91216_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91216'>相逢地，还忆今宵三韭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91216'>青山知了迎候。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91216'>东风自送归帆去，吹得乱红沾袖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91216'>暮云皱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91216'>听杜宇高高，啼向无何有。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91216'>江花垂手。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91216'>任春色重来，江花更好，难可少年又。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91216_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91215?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91215'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91215'>待欲归、家山未得，方知名不如酒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91215'>丹砂便做金勾漏，难遣鬓青似柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91215'>试搔首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91215'>记移竹南塘，又是三年后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91215'>情怀非旧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91215'>叹少日相如，垆边老去，能赋上林否。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91215_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91215'>种兰处，赢得青青种韭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91215'>渊明中路相候。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91215'>何须更待三三径，也自长拖衫袖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91215'>青袍皱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91215'>笑昨醉如泥，盟言止酒，何事醒来又。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91215_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91208?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十八 </span></a><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年</a>　本年陈静山生日，辰翁有词贺。作品：《金缕曲》（昨醉君家酒）<div id='poem_91083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
