id='poem_sentence_3_90947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_90947'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_90947_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年1月</a>　本年游南岗禅寺，作记。作品：《南岗禅寺记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（吴企明《刘辰翁年谱》作3月，当误。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年3月</a>　吉州龙泉县改夫子庙为县学，为之作记。作品：《吉州龙泉县新学记》<div id='poem_1319350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吉州龙泉县新学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319350")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319350'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319350'>天下未尝一日废学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319350_comment'></div>自孝弟日用、君臣上下、历象祭祀、官寺曲直、使客应对、军师名义、市井然信、器服度数，事事物物皆道，事事物物皆学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319350_comment'></div>道何尝一日不行于天下，夫妇之愚由之而不知，学者习焉察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319350_comment'></div>是故以校庠序学，不以无校庠序而不学，而校庠序亦不绝于世者，则长育人才之事，自不得不由此其选耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319350_comment'></div>混一以来，文献次第举，或者遂谓儒生出吏胥、异教下，俎豆不复设，设亦戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319350_comment'></div>会二三廉吏典型相望，闵焉于礼乐之缺失，布德音，厉名教，于是收绮席于园蔬，扶坏壁于马厩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319350_comment'></div>然周爰所不及者其县，县远也，龙泉又远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319350_comment'></div>乃五星聚南斗之明年乙酉三月，龙泉改夫子庙，庙新，学遂滨之，诵曰：「我有夫子，鲁人祀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319350_comment'></div>我有弦歌，嘉宾启之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319350_comment'></div>谁能纪成，千载俟之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319350_comment'></div>则相率具吉水朱簿《请孙氏没官宅为夫子庙状》伻来，愿记其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319350_comment'></div>簿名宪，东平人也，以檄至龙泉，谒殿，圜视门扉斋庐无一有，负城濠，迫江岸，水岁至岁陷，慨然曰：「吾鲁人也，吾不可以不力于夫子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319350_comment'></div>吾尝制诸暨，事夫子如鲁，属邑簿亦有意素定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319350_comment'></div>是日相攸，得孙氏故居金山之麓，夷旷高敞，极四面中，佥曰：「邑何不燬，存是如有待」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319350_comment'></div>朱簿以是驰白郡，如邑请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319350_comment'></div>邑令佐、学官、多士兴起如涌，奉城外迁城中，庚寅舍菜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319350_comment'></div>予披图志状，为诸生叹曰：学官废学有矣，有以遂事兴者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319350_comment'></div>何所为而为之，不可当吾世而废吾邑学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319350_comment'></div>吾邑也，吾兴之可也，异邑之大夫何所为而为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319350_comment'></div>二三子亦知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319350_comment'></div>此夫子所不能得于晚周者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319350_comment'></div>今人惟见衮衣赤舄，万世通祀，以为贤于尧舜之世，不知从其祀者非畏匡之士，则陈蔡之役也，盖圣人之业勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319350_comment'></div>今吾兵革之后，得与周馀幸民閒居无事，咏歌先王之道，又邂逅往来贤人君子拾遗补阙，不惟有绵蕝之观，而又有爽鸠之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319350_comment'></div>大哉居乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319350_comment'></div>此一邑之士所不能得于其盛时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319350_comment'></div>帘垂白日，世短年长，岂无老洫伤坏而抱不用之恨者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319350_comment'></div>毋亦惟是，圣人复起，斯文未丧，身为颜闵，抑何为于此道，未尝不见用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319350_comment'></div>以吾道为不用，则佛氏独得而用之乎，彼无君臣上下者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319350_comment'></div>以吾道为无用，则老氏独得而用之乎，彼重以身为天下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319350_comment'></div>今夫敬忠以临其民，孰非夫子之教，是吾道夐然独立于天地之间，万法之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319350_comment'></div>道用于时，岂必其我？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319350_comment'></div>四时行矣，百物生矣，复欲为于四时百物之外，天厌之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319350_comment'></div>人亦有言，用舍行藏，在舍能藏，惟有道者能之，故曰：「惟我与尔有是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319350_comment'></div>伤夫吾党之无人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319350_comment'></div>是乡俗厚气淳，前修未远，忠信多而甚好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319350_comment'></div>为士此时，惟当灌园以急公上，谨身以训闾巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319350_comment'></div>他年过是邑者，闻有处士之庐，能却城围于三十里，幽居谷口者又隐然名重于京师，素位而行，其必自平时不由径始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319350_comment'></div>不然，道未尝废也，人废之，人未尝废之，士废之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319350_comment'></div>学固未尝不盛也，呜呼，吾于父兄师友至卷卷也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1319350_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e62ccf5f86fa4d6ca2ace087e5661dbc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e62ccf5f86fa4d6ca2ace087e5661dbc");'><span id='e62ccf5f86fa4d6ca2ace087e5661dbc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1287')">1285-1287年</a>，54-56岁</div><div id='e62ccf5f86fa4d6ca2ace087e5661dbc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年9月9日</a>　重阳节登高，有词二首，题曰：“乙酉九日”作品：《南乡子》（宽处略从容）《玉楼春》（龙山歌舞无人道）<div id='poem_91108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南乡子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>乙酉九日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91108")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91108'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91108'>宽处略从容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91108'>华水华山自不同。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91108'>旧日诸贤携手恨，匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91108'>只说明年甚处重。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91108_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91108'>几岁避辽东。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91108'>茅竹秋风一并空。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91108'>欲望辽东何处是，濛濛。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91108'>也似秦楼一梦中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91108_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91012' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91012' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91012?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉楼春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>乙酉九日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91012")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91012'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91012'>龙山歌舞无人道。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91012'>只说先生狂落帽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91012'>秋风亦是可怜人，要令天意知人老。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91012_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91012'>菊花不为重阳早。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91012'>自爱古人诗句恼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91012'>与君郑重说残年，残年惟有重阳好。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_91012_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年</a>　友人邓剡祥兴二年被俘后于本年遣还抵庐陵故乡。此年生日，辰翁有贺词。作品：《洞仙歌》（也曾海上）<div id='poem_91116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91116?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洞仙歌<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>寿中甫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91116")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91116_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91116'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91116'>也曾海上，啖如瓜大枣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91116'>海上归来相公老。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91116'>画堂深、满引明月清风，家山好、一笑尘生蓬岛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91116_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91116'>六年春易过，赢得清阴，到处持杯藉芳草。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91116'>看明年此日，人在黄金台上，早整顿、乾坤事了。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91116'>但细数齐年几人存，更宰相高年，几人能到。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_91116_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年</a>　和李云岩词一首。作品：《百字令》（少微星小）<div id='poem_91026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>百字令<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91026")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91026_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_91026'>李云岩先生远记初度，手写去年赤壁歌，岁晚寄之，少贱不敢当也。匆匆和韵，寄长须去，倘以可教则教之。</div><div id='poem_preface_91026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91026'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91026'>少微星小。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91026'>抚剑气横空，隐见林杪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91026'>夜来宋都如雨，更长得奇哉懰皎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91026'>与汝三龄，览余初度，一语占先兆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91026'>暮年喜见，甲申聚五星照。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91026_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91026'>堪叹亡国馀民，老人孺子，尔汝霜桥晓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91026'>骑马听鸡朝寂寞，梦入南枝三绕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91026'>洛社耆英，行窝真率，著我真堪笑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91026_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91026'>与公试数，开禧嘉定宝绍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_91026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年7月</a>　为庐陵万安县舜祠写买田记。作品：《万安县舜祠买田记》<div id='poem_1319364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>万安县舜祠买田记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319364")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319364'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319364'>大州僻邑，深山小寺，而一日揭焉以舜祠兴，虽邈乎褊矣，然能使周旋博雅之士为之矫首而遐思，汎滥游骛之人为之褰裳而忘倦，亦其所立有在常情之表者，则宝祐、景定间僧了敬之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319364_comment'></div>方祠未成，记先具，乡绣衣持节至其处问焉，见其画堵基山为读书室，虽嘉其有志，若寓言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319364_comment'></div>又久之堂成祠成，祠成而敬去主龙须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319364_comment'></div>其徒慈意者自仰山归嗣敬，嗣敬之十五年而买田既百馀石，合是二百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319364_comment'></div>敬来求田记刻寺，俾有考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319364_comment'></div>余笑曰：时节世间，安得不使来者笑，人无能何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319364_comment'></div>昔之舜祠者成之难，而今之寺田者获之易也，则亦有闻舜祠之风者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319364_comment'></div>如将为尔并舜祠记之耶，则或者以为无谓也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319364_comment'></div>不并尔舜祠记之，又未有知夫无谓之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319364_comment'></div>寺在韶山，山之下为韶江，江韶口，里韶濩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319364_comment'></div>虽俚讹志谬，自儒者言之无一可，若在彼教中，古帝王亦犹幻耳，悟则舜在床琴，不悟则陟方乃死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319364_comment'></div>吾以韶山见舜，事舜如吾师，然乡人士之为我来者如邺侯书堂，如李氏山房，士大夫之过其下者如望苍梧，登九成，要亦何以大相过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319364_comment'></div>荒滨绝径，诡为异闻，隐为奇观，游者如有所慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319364_comment'></div>因徘徊之久，而又有感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319364_comment'></div>向之田者始由是而积矣，人有常言，曰知自孰知，田之自舜又孰知，日用饮食、父子兄弟无一之非舜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319364_comment'></div>斯民异端，无重华故至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319364_comment'></div>今夫山田二百，井田之世不足当上农夫二人之食，然亦有甚难者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319364_comment'></div>今夫耕者或不得食，贩夫夜作，旦而市，或不售则不食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319364_comment'></div>彼深山大众，不耕不售，而不缺食，不惟不缺，复有馀，而田者积焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319364_comment'></div>今夫望施于人难矣，有得有不得焉，再而竭，三而倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319364_comment'></div>或不得谢则怨，而施之佛者即甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319364_comment'></div>如梁萧氏以其国则小，果然施者常不悔也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319364_comment'></div>不惟不悔，益腆而田者积焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319364_comment'></div>彼岂能皆一生死，齐得丧，道隆行显，且佛实有力至此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319364_comment'></div>乃其迂阔则又若舜祠者焉，岂非心胸眉目复有在福田之外，莫之致而至，而好德者远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319364_comment'></div>山无穷，田无穷，百年千年连阡陌始此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319364_comment'></div>夫舜祠者理之所不当有，而佛之所无用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319364_comment'></div>固有有之，而不事事之，而犹无益，而二僧以此为无穷，且以此不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319364_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319364_comment'></div>昔者万安、永福何至此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319364_comment'></div>后舜祠二十三年七月，须溪记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1319364_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年9月9日</a>　本年重阳节有词。作品：《金缕曲》（风雨东篱晚）<div id='poem_91064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金缕曲<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十七 </span>丙戌九日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91064")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91064'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91064'>风雨东篱晚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91064'>渺人间、南北东西，平芜烟远。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91064'>旧日携壶吹帽处，一色沉冥何限。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91064'>天不遣、魂消肠断。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91064'>不是苦无看山分，料青山、也自羞人面。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91064'>秋后瘦，老来倦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91064_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91064'>惊回昨梦青山转。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91064'>恨一林、金粟都空，静无人见。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91064'>默默黄花明朝有，只待插花寻伴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91064'>又谁笑、今朝蝶怨。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91064'>潦倒玉山休重醉，到簪萸、忍待人频劝。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91064_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91064'>今又惜，几人健。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_91064_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年12月</a>　本月死于二月份的丁守廉下葬，为之写墓志铭。作品：《丁守廉墓志铭》<div id='poem_1319402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁守廉墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319402")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319402'>士不幸而用所学于科举，其得失饥渴、升沉胜败曾不如庶人之常业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319402_comment'></div>虽有宽易静笃之君子，十上五黜，幸不黜，愈恨恨乃甚于黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319402_comment'></div>使夫怜伤太息者犹惑于其命，则所以烦瞀摧废当何如，而益退然确然，死而浩然，盖夺精失营者莫科举之为累，而其阨穷不闷者必学道之有得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319402_comment'></div>余于记礼家老儒丁守廉之葬，若不知时世之已易，慨然道之如新，亦士之不幸，舍此无可言者，复于斯墓也不知何云，吾犹独为斯墓恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319402_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319402_comment'></div>科目之负人也多矣，由今言之，亦何恨于科目哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319402_comment'></div>口授之徒，心相似之友，今年某某荐，明年某某第，又明年如某年，或喜曰：「桷榱收，梁栋宜有待」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319402_comment'></div>或喟曰：「广岂不当侯，不侯」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319402_comment'></div>君曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319402_comment'></div>吾先鞭为有人矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319402_comment'></div>当丙午，犹朝日也，揭焉而首选，不及送；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319402_comment'></div>戊午且四十矣，再选辄再屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319402_comment'></div>已而甲子复然，甲子至癸酉复然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319402_comment'></div>问谁贡，贡二人止，往往门弟子而止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319402_comment'></div>吾州多士贡额多临江数倍，每榜后，考者为言某卷得复失，能使人出狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319402_comment'></div>况一经屡试，白首洴澼，学虽吾事，而世貌哗名，殉者成路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319402_comment'></div>观其死之前日，犹明窗就晓，抄书自课如儿子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319402_comment'></div>死之日，复大书示其子云：「死非所畏，何必张皇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319402_comment'></div>学问不衰，死生不变」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319402_comment'></div>又实有得如此，其视往年场屋间梦，不类芥鸡之相践而木鸡之微视耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319402_comment'></div>然昔之怜伤太息者至是犹不置，则书生之清论，世道之遗思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319402_comment'></div>君之子敬直脩谨有礼，称其家声，屡至请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319402_comment'></div>凡求铭其先者，苟不得志于利达，必鄙绝科目，自附前辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319402_comment'></div>余嘉敬直用意真，取名浅，又见高安辛拱辰叙其同门受业身通者以十数，且云先生贫而介，视富贵人无足动其意，无妄言笑，乡党穆然敬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319402_comment'></div>其自叙殖礼斋则云：先大父潜山先生出蜀，载书数千卷，曰：「使吾子孙免为俗子之归，亦免为势家所夺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319402_comment'></div>繇是自号殖礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319402_comment'></div>以学殖易货殖，惩训严甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319402_comment'></div>潜山事庆元诸老，犹及章云山、叶水心、刘后溪，如杨西岩恢、项云叟寅孙辈又其徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319402_comment'></div>义理浸淫，有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319402_comment'></div>近见其《礼记集解》三十卷手藁，如虫蚀叶，盖老是经者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319402_comment'></div>初名里，字守廉，晚犹称守廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319402_comment'></div>世居西江新喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319402_comment'></div>曾祖公逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319402_comment'></div>祖居易，绍熙进士，奉议郎、宰宜春，潜山先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319402_comment'></div>父昱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319402_comment'></div>生嘉定庚辰，年六十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319402_comment'></div>娶欧阳氏，子四人：敬直、行直、养直、友直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319402_comment'></div>养直以丙子走间道省亲，遇兵死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319402_comment'></div>孙男二：本度、复春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319402_comment'></div>社山其祖墓也，距家二里，祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319402_comment'></div>其卒以丙戌二月，葬以十二月丙申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319402_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1319402'>贡不贡，为槐梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319402_comment'></div>丘盖多，于讴诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319402_comment'></div>羿之彀，而不中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319402_comment'></div>名淹中，何必用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319402_comment'></div>涕斯沾，安致凤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1319402_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　卒于十月的萧寿甫年底下葬，为之写墓志铭。作品：《萧寿甫墓志铭》<div id='poem_1319403' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319403' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319403?labeling=true' target='_blank'>萧寿甫墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319403")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319403_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319403'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319403'>曩学禁时，海内名号未起，吾庐陵之南、须山之北有大儒先生曰黄宗鲁，其子为叔豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319403_comment'></div>吾先人师宗鲁而友叔豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319403_comment'></div>叔豹以文名六馆，接庆元诸老，自是从吾先人游者彬彬如二黄间，而朱氏甥父子实先后，诸生复转授为资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319403_comment'></div>余七八岁时，表氏抱余学，称尧章先生，后改名埴，字圣匋，号古平，官至太学博士，倅袁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319403_comment'></div>如西昌萧寿父大德少圣匋一岁耳，于时事圣匋如弟子，又以弟子俱见吾先人，先人厚之如厚吾出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319403_comment'></div>先人死，吾十岁，概未尝知其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319403_comment'></div>晚而圣匋以赋奏南宫第一，又甲科，其名位之兴，赫然欲揭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319403_comment'></div>当年叔豹，上士争相藉寄，自谓出朱氏门下，师其父者亦诡得师其子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319403_comment'></div>乃寿父则未尝知其人，而其人亦莫之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319403_comment'></div>此布衣师友之略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319403_comment'></div>日寿父死，而其子来泣曰：「芳春之登门晚，若吾父之登门则不可谓不早也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319403_comment'></div>今吾子恺又馆于朱教古平子之子，是斯文四世之泽如泉脉脉，往往自公家始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319403_comment'></div>幸存弟子世家，示万世子孙毋忘其初」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319403_comment'></div>予以其言笃厚系流风，又知寿父朴茂似前辈，虽其存若不愿人知者，不当为众人道，乃其所以可称者，亦不能不为众人道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319403_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319403_comment'></div>其忍不铭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319403_comment'></div>余以德祐岁逃空虚，干戈反覆之交，望萧氏秋岭如一叶，凡流离接境者必此焉依而后得宁宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319403_comment'></div>已而盗四起，已而官军北方，且为风林，为疑帜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319403_comment'></div>然盗过之曰毋犯，官倚之掎而角，喜之者以为造物之报，而君子则归之德言之著，云：乡人之至于斗者，重其言如季路、季布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319403_comment'></div>或陷于义，众推户削迹，甚者希购市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319403_comment'></div>雍容亲党之间，无怨无怵，勉其子尽力，友赖以完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319403_comment'></div>此其事在近年耳目者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319403_comment'></div>平生执贽如其邑之温帅干英臣、乡先达敖适轩、陈念斋、陈静斋，所交杨景尧、蔡济父、陈鸣道、萧清父、康行可，或得之隐约，或托之岁寒，相敬爱终其身，非以其六七贵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319403_comment'></div>尝试场屋，不大效即弃去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319403_comment'></div>所校雠把玩，愈老愈笃，子孙多所严事，而自教者居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319403_comment'></div>襟怀春意，见于日涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319403_comment'></div>嗜酒好客，力有不足，而性尝有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319403_comment'></div>吾虽不及识，如见其人，如闻其语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319403_comment'></div>况以吾童子时先人之好徵吾言千载，而吾于古平复自有兄弟师友之谊，于古平之所教如古平焉，故曰如见其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319403_comment'></div>寿父号静安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319403_comment'></div>其死以丙戌十月十九日，曰：「鸡鸣吾行矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319403_comment'></div>鸡鸣而逝，年七十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319403_comment'></div>曾祖某，祖某，父某，娶某，子孙婿某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319403_comment'></div>是年某月甲子葬某乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319403_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1319403'>有冠而后有緌，有苓而后有丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319403_comment'></div>孰谢其蓝，箕以传箕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319403_comment'></div>繄教父谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319403_comment'></div>父父是思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319403_comment'></div>式谷尔孙，稷而食之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1319403_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　新喻县学重修大成殿，为之作记。作品：《临江军新喻县学重修大成殿记》<div id='poem_1319284' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319284' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319284?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江军新喻县学重修大成殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319284")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319284_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319284'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319284'>喻学丙戌之修礼殿，为大教官吴凤孙以丁学谕敬直来请曰：「老生无能为于乡党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319284_comment'></div>视前楹碑，吾宋绍定戊子李侯仁任所修也，于今六十年矣，柱崩梁坏，风雨岿然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319284_comment'></div>乃乙酉十月，廉部真定赵公秉政，既定先圣弟子籍百又二十人，复其终身，常调不征，县旌别有加，命修学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319284_comment'></div>于是令丞簿尉各以其力为倡，士之经营劝相者奔走来会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319284_comment'></div>月三望而功毕，广辟丈馀，灵星翼张，越佚贯旧，夐焉出于震荡残缺之后，盖劳于创造而大于兴继，凤孙则承乏视成而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319284_comment'></div>此部使者奉宣之实意，而诸大夫邑人受学之大谊也，于念兹敢请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319284_comment'></div>余惟是邑名公多士非猥远凡陋者之所敢及，既辞不获让，则受言载之于篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319284_comment'></div>道犹天也，凡干戈溃乱之出于宇宙，如雷霆风雨，危不可处，而天体霁然，不待明日，光复其旧，必归于礼乐情性、道德风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319284_comment'></div>如使古圣人之所以为天下国家者不用，而一出于兵与刑，则民之类灭久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319284_comment'></div>孰非命也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319284_comment'></div>繇周公而上，千有馀岁，命世而为君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319284_comment'></div>繇孔子至今，亦千有馀岁，命世而为儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319284_comment'></div>君道未尝非儒，儒者实辅是君以明其道，故诵尧之言，行尧之行，是亦尧而已矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319284_comment'></div>诵夫子之言，行夫子之行，是亦夫子而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319284_comment'></div>居敬行简，以临其民，南面之夫子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319284_comment'></div>敬事而信，节用爱人，千乘之夫子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319284_comment'></div>一日无是道，则国非其国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319284_comment'></div>而儒者犹歉然曰不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319284_comment'></div>道未尝不用于世，而世有无用之儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319284_comment'></div>代之所以绝续存亡，民之所以死生利病，特系于理之是非，而不在其人之用舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319284_comment'></div>得乎道而为天，得乎天而为命，道、命一物也，古今一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319284_comment'></div>道在是则夫子在是，夫子在是则君道在是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319284_comment'></div>故事道如夫子，事夫子如事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319284_comment'></div>《记》曰：「能为师而后能为长，能为长而后能为君」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319284_comment'></div>夫子教为君者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319284_comment'></div>律有烦有省，令有迁有改，惟经之为训毋敢畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319284_comment'></div>是故《春秋》者，拨乱反正，万世太平之书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319284_comment'></div>利欲之横流也甚于洪水，然平成之后，不闻复有洪水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319284_comment'></div>由今之俗，望春秋犹治世，非春秋之世治也，所以为春秋者治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319284_comment'></div>刑之而有不惩也，兵之而有不遏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319284_comment'></div>君君臣臣父父子子受之天为中国，受之王为嘉师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319284_comment'></div>必有推明人极之立与天地并，其效常得于世教之所不及，而后知今之致隆者容有未尽，昔之暂废者本未尝亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319284_comment'></div>夫视学告朔，岂直观美哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319284_comment'></div>诸生低回习礼，具瞻冕服，其亦思夫东家之匹夫，陈蔡之环辙，时君遗之，乡国违之，而所以致此者，亦其遁世无闷、不怨不尤、屈于一时者，为教大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319284_comment'></div>故必以迂晦为世守，阨穷为家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319284_comment'></div>而况上之人优重之，作成之，当路简擢之，著定之，阖邑茂异之，顾其踽踽凉凉，一或不能专志于道，而终安于命，则所以为天下国家者又未见其有可望，而天下国家亦卒若外之者，未必皆世之咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319284_comment'></div>余既言三代馀民受罔极之赐如夫子者，又欲陋巷时贤以身之贫贱学其为夫子者，盖进取之事不在科举，而在学术与人品，此世道之古也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1319284_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年3月</a>　友人黄纯父卒，葬于三月，为之写墓志铭。作品：《黄纯父墓志铭》<div id='poem_1319401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄纯父墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319401")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319401'>岁庚辰，予初与纯父遇风雪东湖之上，惊相吊曰：「贾鹿泉见君文，问古人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319401_comment'></div>今人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319401_comment'></div>或者亦以君为古矣，君在此耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319401_comment'></div>语杂悲喜，至甚夜不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319401_comment'></div>未明复撼予语，拊髀浩然曰：「吾平生慕汤东涧，近年慕君，亦欲从君后耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319401_comment'></div>君岂从古心公致误耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319401_comment'></div>识君慷慨，叙寄不浅，因拥衾而起，以所闻于江先生者为君言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319401_comment'></div>如东涧何可及也，未第时，与其兄客徐景说，标致已不相合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319401_comment'></div>既第，待信州户阙，一日有赵尚书出参赞督府，视事，首见簿姓名，叹曰：「余识之，真西山时汤某乃犹为此官哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319401_comment'></div>即拜疏荐之，代主象山，从是隐然出徐径畈上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319401_comment'></div>自端平至景定三年，出入诸老，皆成履历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319401_comment'></div>即小人扳引，及当国所忌恶，皆不足为全名之累，不待辩某事、忤某人，而大节自不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319401_comment'></div>此如陈太丘、黄叔度，公论常身为之地，故树立矫矫，不肯为人称门生也，亦各其时命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319401_comment'></div>言未既，君泪沾余衾，独举往年麻姑山梦，梦一籍题「忠孝」二字，而某在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319401_comment'></div>孝不敢言也，忠特若此，予亦喟然，于少年州县不自试一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319401_comment'></div>因举子房，天授沛公，他多疑拒，独县悟如子房意，此所谓汉事将成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319401_comment'></div>诵《出师表》，至「引喻失义，以垂忠谏」，想见庸人自用，故伤心玄德之不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319401_comment'></div>身世何长，今人喜言四方上下，孰知言不见奇，奇而不用，不用而验，验而悔，悔而恨，恨且见祸，其进退偪仄，复非前古君臣之比哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319401_comment'></div>君曰：「世事勿复言，即文字何等不足存，而魏郑公以此，杨大年以此，憾至死」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319401_comment'></div>因泛论邺侯山人高致，魏延与淮阴胆略相似，李伯纪、张魏公成败天意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319401_comment'></div>语不必有出，出不必有谓，未尝及心事，彼此直歔欷往复，不知出于君之口与余口也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319401_comment'></div>于是相知深矣，复欲与君谈，不可得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319401_comment'></div>前年犹寄余诗，去年有持书来，视缄题若不可识，则君死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319401_comment'></div>余以岁初谢客，呜咽而入问，耿兰以故至，举扶病中相属语，肠痛欲绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319401_comment'></div>海内人物风流略尽，托君笔墨相荫映，后死犹有讲学之望，顾不乐人间世如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319401_comment'></div>念前冬有沅湘老人以君文求余记曰：「黄先生虽不能饮，尚健坐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319401_comment'></div>余谓纯父长七尺，年五十，生世大有事在，迄如此而止，造物复何以我辈为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319401_comment'></div>读门人状君行，岂不整密婉至，然不如君前夕剧谈尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319401_comment'></div>予著君语语，而俯仰浩荡，人物著微，心迹缠绵，功名蹉跌，后有君子，可以想见而叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319401_comment'></div>若状所难言，又有人不及知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319401_comment'></div>江阃贵人与边守将不相接，君代书密付，语见赤心，指授得宜，又多军情所郁不得达者，繇是感泣思效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319401_comment'></div>仓猝用意，胜谢东山自异，顾内幕所左右能此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319401_comment'></div>其苦言节费，见于赏募得淮卒三千备游击，为淮捷营；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319401_comment'></div>改铁鹞小船为艨艟大舰取胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319401_comment'></div>议诸郡闭绝流民如他盗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319401_comment'></div>请城外筑堡居老弱，而各选其壮者从军便；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319401_comment'></div>为阃帅释当路之怨，驰从约之书，共图国忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319401_comment'></div>胸怀磊磊，出于人所不望，而人亦知惟君所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319401_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319401_comment'></div>使君得乘一障，亦当远胜一阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319401_comment'></div>虽九江事去，相府逋虚，诸司蒙茸，君犹力勉以私财招军，抚溪峒为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319401_comment'></div>至独松失守，庚牌暮下速援，行者议饶、信道梗，盍径崇安绕出三衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319401_comment'></div>兵夜发，君与家人不相顾，至石门遇长幼相泣，君曰：「国事至此，暇顾尔辈耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319401_comment'></div>自是言之有伤心者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319401_comment'></div>国家养兵三百年，体群臣，子庶民，三宫仁俭，一朝有难，人怀顾望，徒拥乌合，盗府库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319401_comment'></div>君以书生，志气感动，言必称君父乃尔，然至旴而旴闭，入闽而闽溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1319401_comment'></div>旴城闭，有投击城下至毙者，诸将欲屠之，君正色不可，曰：「我辈以路梗假道致疑耳，若屠一城，三宫闻必震骇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1319401_comment'></div>诸将已瞋目谋不利，君不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1319401_comment'></div>既又具军行宿次启奏，有笑者曰：「君犹谓有通进所耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1319401_comment'></div>君慨然泣下，曰：「诚不忍以为无也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1319401_comment'></div>闻者始掩涕叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1319401_comment'></div>及入闽，有狠将以衣粮乏，咄咄谋劫主帅以出，语已逼，君又不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1319401_comment'></div>一日坐水阁，有飞矢掠项过著柱，迹所由来，忌君者出此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1319401_comment'></div>明日君行，军亦溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1319401_comment'></div>生乱世，无及于救，又不自为政，故所就止尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1319401_comment'></div>然积诚所至，在建而劝分分，建昌而祈雨雨，皆以客馆系人望，得天意，亦何尝有一日得行其志，而惜之者如已试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1319401_comment'></div>世自有尽，君名方兴，有西园八十之老傅太史自得以君来，为赋诗，喜曰：「碑无庞老名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1319401_comment'></div>又曰：「能威兵处在真诚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1319401_comment'></div>其志虑风采何如也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1319401_comment'></div>自咸淳第，授静江府临桂簿，尝辟泗州淮平尉，不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1319401_comment'></div>后五年，辟建康府凤台酒库，自是始与幕议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1319401_comment'></div>又五年，辟临安府德清酒库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1319401_comment'></div>德祐初，差干办江西制司，复带行礼兵架阁，未几复带行国子正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1319401_comment'></div>明年除宗正簿、督机，特改宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1319401_comment'></div>初筮，交代违年，不愿上，仍待阙淮平界北，得遥授，曰：「不敢欺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1319401_comment'></div>及登畿，有衔命钩致者，自免径归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1319401_comment'></div>诸司举削，常片纸书所闻廉介有政声者，请以己所应得者举之，受举者不知也，或知而谢，辄避去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1319401_comment'></div>此事亦近年所罕见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1319401_comment'></div>余出仕十五年，未尝受人一削，君自谓出处与余同，谓此自其父得闻象山之学于其诸大父，益贯彻朱陆，授学者恳恻穷至，所至老成钦动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1319401_comment'></div>诸所识予不能尽知，而尤于丹徒陆君实秀夫耿耿焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1319401_comment'></div>君实大节可哀，君实文不多见，见君文，识君实，宜君实之所纳贽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1319401_comment'></div>君文不蹈袭诸作，不为时文、议论、讲义、注疏，而辞事义理俱至，清整酣畅，足自为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1319401_comment'></div>诗亦有思致，竭目前意，朴厚雅驯，视他人能此复少彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1319401_comment'></div>至于家庭讲授，人物大意，伦纪亲切，廪廪见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1319401_comment'></div>千峰陈公宗礼尝对人云：「吾欲得一客如黄纯父清苦，不可得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1319401_comment'></div>其文之有本又如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1319401_comment'></div>士常患不第，一第足自致，谊能以去就易民命，争国事，彼权倖险奸、贪懦狠僭，辞能辟，意能诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1319401_comment'></div>世狭道迂，而环辙如陪臣，坐膑如车中，及其穷蹙无能，有甚于鲁男子之不得去而南霁云之不能食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1319401_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1319401_comment'></div>微斯人，斯世之不幸，斯言也亦孰知其可悲！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1319401_comment'></div>君临川黄氏，居崇仁东里，讳丙炎，初字文炳，晚更字汉翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1319401_comment'></div>予诔之曰纯父，其乡称之曰思梅先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1319401_comment'></div>生丙申，卒丙戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1319401_comment'></div>曾祖俨，祖邦基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1319401_comment'></div>父应辰，梅窗公也，思梅，思公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1319401_comment'></div>妣陈夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1319401_comment'></div>娶陈氏，子男六：庆孙、兴孙、凤孙、翼孙、晖孙、慈老，翼孙继姻党陈，慈老以治命后，凤孙、庆孙笔墨可爱，皆如思梅复生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1319401_comment'></div>婿赵次愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1319401_comment'></div>孙男五，女二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1319401_comment'></div>葬崇仁乡西隐里雷公山，实丁亥三月丙午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1319401_comment'></div>君厚重不妄语，疏阔无馀怀，及所委曲倾尽若自营，收致后进有豪气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1319401_comment'></div>乙丑自京归安仁，道中有盗杀人逸，累居者，既诬服，君以过客得盗名，告使者，使者得实，谢曰：「君乍脱场屋，洗冤如此，可量哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1319401_comment'></div>其后避难，得便舟，出溪洞，各护送，皆所尝尽力有恩意者，亦若有助焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1319401_comment'></div>乃铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_1319401'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1319401_comment'></div>国之初也，材不必其如君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1319401_comment'></div>世之甚也，忧不必其如臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1319401_comment'></div>莫不幸于以身从人，又不幸而以文致身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1319401_comment'></div>故虽有孔明、公瑾，而用之如陈琳、阮瑀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1319401_comment'></div>又如温、石二子，而不得为许远与张巡，岂非命云！</div><div id='poem_sentence_98_1319401_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4159db34245c4a07b94c73087209cf2d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4159db34245c4a07b94c73087209cf2d");'><span id='4159db34245c4a07b94c73087209cf2d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1295')">1287-1295年</a>，56-64岁</div><div id='4159db34245c4a07b94c73087209cf2d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年</a>　僧绍隆请居空相院废居，为之作记。作品：《空相院记》<div id='poem_1319292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>空相院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319292")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319292'>佛以一麻一麦兴，而为其徒者皆安受人施，至撞钟伐鼓，列食万钵，号称禅林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319292_comment'></div>其下者犹说缘说果，致俗倾信，如食租衣税，又不耕食，又不幸水旱，然犹不失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319292_comment'></div>未有受田于人而空夺于官府，几废寺不赡，日求于无何有以待还定者二十有七年，如吾庐陵曲濑之空相院者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319292_comment'></div>至其克复旧物，则又难于天雨而苦于日辟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319292_comment'></div>盖彼失而我复之为戒，后人虽欲不记，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319292_comment'></div>院不知起何年，而赐额治平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319292_comment'></div>又不知何年何许萧氏舍田百石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319292_comment'></div>人世长短不可知，以三十年为一世，计僧几腊，萧几世，绝续又未可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319292_comment'></div>会有他杨攘袂起曰：「吾祖尝施是，敢以上学官而增贡士庄籍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319292_comment'></div>繇是没入如卷地尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319292_comment'></div>院于此时，所有独治平额耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319292_comment'></div>有僧绍隆得大法，忍甘受其苦，爰贷爰粥，慨然曰：「吾屋不脩且废」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319292_comment'></div>众谓无田不废亦废，岁敝岁脩，万缘难备，僧佛共依，指廪何俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319292_comment'></div>起戊午，历丙子，而贡士庄亦废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319292_comment'></div>废且十年，隆冒霜露，敝衣缕，顶天而额地，曰：「士复安取此」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319292_comment'></div>郡以例如其请，归之，甫前年乙酉事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319292_comment'></div>壁则故壁，而隆亦老且病矣，惩曰：「是田也，坏于寺兄弟之不协，而后间者托焉，非施夺异也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319292_comment'></div>乃合云散，收雁序，戒尚腊白，传次灯叶，混然大同，业习一空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319292_comment'></div>又以其铢积众施者为田可八十石合于前，如干不私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319292_comment'></div>其更事老人顾而叹曰：「施易得也，耕易穫也，孰能饥腹以待人之馀饱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319292_comment'></div>孰能取之其怀而不堕甑弃以及此」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319292_comment'></div>须溪居士问之，笑曰：「然，然非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319292_comment'></div>众生寿者必起于人我，我故彼，彼非我，不争故我为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319292_comment'></div>若平其心以平不平之物，似矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319292_comment'></div>平者其谁与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319292_comment'></div>非我之我与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319292_comment'></div>今夫得田以遗子孙，惟恐其不多也，是众生相也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319292_comment'></div>又惟恐其不久也，是寿者相也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319292_comment'></div>当其得时，贪认己有，展转必至，诸将并生，如尔所争，复从舍起，今复谁舍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319292_comment'></div>斛百几何，代阅废兴，指冢为薪，芳臭同尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319292_comment'></div>长荒凉乏绝而不困者独此心耳，而此心亦我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319292_comment'></div>夫知物之空矣，而我犹在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319292_comment'></div>是田也，非我则不复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319292_comment'></div>未复我责，既复我忘，萧然付之，无町无畦，见争者之非我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319292_comment'></div>既又慊然曰：「由我而复，则亦未忘之我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319292_comment'></div>夫知我之空矣，而空空者犹在也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319292_comment'></div>于是老隆失然而起曰：「院名空相，非空空相，法法皆尽，惟记独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319292_comment'></div>是空空已，空相不空」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319292_comment'></div>居士点头：如是如是。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1319292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年</a>　本年友人刘达仲卒，为之作墓志铭。作品：《乐邱处士墓志铭》<div id='poem_1319406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐丘处士墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319406")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319406'>安成古长沙郡，吾庐陵之刘未尝不本长沙也，而谱多不可考，多故不可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319406_comment'></div>按《唐思禅师塔碑》，思刘氏，长沙定王后，是为七祖，而龙须山担岭二塔化身相望，皆其家兄弟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319406_comment'></div>他日见石勋、石材、石砻三庙，亦兄弟，思同祖云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319406_comment'></div>而安成有兴泰刘氏神者，又长沙来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319406_comment'></div>荒山野水之间，时时出于残碑断系如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319406_comment'></div>吾故家在须山之阳，而祖墓在担岭之下，尝欲考而同之，嫌其特出于往往不可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319406_comment'></div>今安成西四十五里曰汤市，有何年处士墓，由湖南徙家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319406_comment'></div>自处士失其名以下，至可仕字达仲凡十世皆可考，则庐陵自汉以来为一刘，益信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319406_comment'></div>达仲有子翼甫尝铭同姓之墓曰：郡士族半刘，宜刘吾乡，而欧吾乡者俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319406_comment'></div>其论可谓伟异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319406_comment'></div>然不知长沙一本，其流溢于东南者皆非某氏比也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319406_comment'></div>虽后来阔远，有他赐姓，亦如士范、蔡墨所言，然终不得与安成比，安成古长沙为近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319406_comment'></div>达仲，乐丘翁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319406_comment'></div>余尝记乐丘，知其贤且达，已记之后三年而乐丘翁死，年七十，乡人士惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319406_comment'></div>是年翼甫又死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319406_comment'></div>其中子应登将以丁亥某月日葬乐丘，请曰：「应登与弟及门旧也，而弟已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319406_comment'></div>知乐丘者记也，葬乐丘以此记可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319406_comment'></div>顾家庭庸行，有记所不及而宜书者，愿并志而铭之，则幽明之望也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319406_comment'></div>余惟是父是子今人间所少，其所言槩常事，而得古人史传语意，此自可传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319406_comment'></div>吾传之以其子应登之言曰：吾翁庶祖母罗氏出也，而后嫡兄暨祖父死，父死，而庶弟怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319406_comment'></div>翁曰：「吾惟不能逃祖父命以及此，今逊可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319406_comment'></div>举惟其弟所欲，而兴受其所不取，间者愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319406_comment'></div>先墓之葬舍南且岁久，相者曰水，启视之不验，卒改葬三十里而近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319406_comment'></div>然终其身以为恨，每对客持杯，呼孙温卷，偶语及此，则潸然不可仰视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319406_comment'></div>生母再殡，病不能送，恸为绝，凡当祭与适墓，呜咽如新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319406_comment'></div>藏先世故书敝履谨，远亲执友下至阍仆异视之有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319406_comment'></div>割产为众祀，岁兴发捐直，籍贫者赋与之，或籍而不至，莫夜歉焉不能食，以为怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319406_comment'></div>甃夷道，焚负券，即郡有守望阡陌之事，必翁也乃可保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319406_comment'></div>故开庆移民，咸淳覈赋，公私无后患馀责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319406_comment'></div>尤多材略，屡兴作，所指画必不可改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319406_comment'></div>应变尤审，忧世若己责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319406_comment'></div>教其子有身法，毋以奇险擅鸣，曰为文不当尔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319406_comment'></div>应凤甲戌条对第五，得建昌判官，驰书预戒，以姑取教官，毋未习与人郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319406_comment'></div>虽书至已授选，而言不可废，故传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319406_comment'></div>阅世俛仰，尤戒远葬、僻葬、险葬、利葬、讼葬，乐丘其所自卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319406_comment'></div>癸未春，廉使滏阳马德昌以乡饮召应登、应凤，问翁日用，大书「乐丘」二字寄，亡恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319406_comment'></div>予读应登行述，至「须髯音吐，左顾稍下，乐丘抱合状，高下茅屋，皆夕阳人影，如见其人，践其处」，叹曰：是能言者，复何以余铭记为！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319406_comment'></div>应登之从曾祖通直公梦才字乘可，嘉熙戊戌第，力学博文，清若有志行，号巢林先生，暮年无子在侧，惟达仲能左右，无细大谋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319406_comment'></div>作本亭于八世祖墓下，买田立石，皆其馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319406_comment'></div>汤村古安复城，水北城隍庙故在，刘氏墓号五处士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319406_comment'></div>处士生珫，珫生赞，赞生继文，继文生臻，臻生士昌，士昌生师望，师望生继，继生克正，克正生三德，三德生有俊，有俊生可仕，是为乐丘，一号桂林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319406_comment'></div>生嘉定丙子十一月二十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319406_comment'></div>娶罗氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319406_comment'></div>三子：应牛、应登、应凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319406_comment'></div>登，江西漕进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319406_comment'></div>翼甫，凤也，见别志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1319406_comment'></div>二女，六孙，十二孙女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1319406_comment'></div>乐丘在其乡永福里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1319406_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1319406'>斯丘之上兮拱木皆春，斯丘之下兮乐友古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1319406_comment'></div>不仰愧而俯怍兮，初返乎吾贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1319406_comment'></div>百世之下犹百世之上兮，其复得为晋无怀葛天氏之民。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1319406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　居家庐陵。作品：《摸鱼儿》（也何须晴如那日）<div id='poem_91211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十七 </span>水东桃花下赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91211")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91211'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91211'>也何须、晴如那日，欣然且过江去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91211'>玄都纵有看花便，耿耿自羞前度。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91211'>堪恨处。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91211'>人道是，漫山先落坡翁句。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91211'>东风绮语。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91211'>但适意当前，来寻须赋，此土亦吾圃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91211_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91211'>海山石，犹记芙蓉城主。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91211'>弹过飞种成土。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91211'>是间便做仙客杏，谁与一栽千树。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91211'>朝又暮。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91211'>怅二十五年，临路花如故。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91211'>人生自苦。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91211'>只唤渡观桃，侵寻至此，世事奈何许。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91211_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　临川尚学林来访，逢生日，为之作词贺寿。作品：《减字木兰花》（相州锦好）<div id='poem_91162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91162?labeling=true' target='_blank'>减字木兰花<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>尚学林己丑寿旦，适归庐陵。其先世相州人，居永和，今家临川</a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91162")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91162_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91162'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91162'>相州锦好。待到相州人已老。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91162'>颍水归田。白鹭惊猜已十年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91162_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91162'>太师尚父。晚遇明时方用武。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91162'>大笑相逢。把酒家乡是客中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91162'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_91162_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　居家庐陵。作品：《岂畦记》《大梵寺记》<div id='poem_1319375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>岂畦记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319375")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319375'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319375'>天地间无息壤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319375_comment'></div>南湖朱氏子得其一丘以为畦，东至于郓欢龟阴，西至于虞芮，南至邬刘蔿于，北至苏忿生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319375_comment'></div>有槔焉，灌之不受，有桑于此，逊又逊之，而莫知其何人也，则相视而笑曰：「子岂畦者耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319375_comment'></div>遂自号岂畦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319375_comment'></div>吾辟之曰：子以不畦之畦，畦人于无所可畦，而立乎其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319375_comment'></div>中者圭也，圭者二土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319375_comment'></div>自南北观之，其何畦何不畦之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319375_comment'></div>开阡囊括以来，宋之揠，楚之蹊岩戈锡之荒不论，论其譬于道者，区以别矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319375_comment'></div>高者为麻麦，下者为蔬芋，数之不能终其物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319375_comment'></div>而陈者皆迹也，变者皆道也，此不足而彼有馀，则吾亦无不足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319375_comment'></div>善种者不穫，善取者常无穷焉，盖无适而非吾畦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319375_comment'></div>人之言曰：鼠壤有馀蔬而弃妹，释者至曲为之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319375_comment'></div>不知至人者自藏于畔侧，遗秉滞穗皆寡妇之利，鼠有馀则妹在其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319375_comment'></div>妹吾妹则爱之，爱焉而不获者众，此望人之腹所以觏而多责也，可不谓哀邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319375_comment'></div>古之夏畦者吾得数人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319375_comment'></div>子产以蕞尔郑为一畦，而人谤之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319375_comment'></div>有莘之野，启七十里为一畦，而匹夫匹妇皆己责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319375_comment'></div>《禹贡》、《周官》至以九州之内则壤经野为一大畦，故胼胝吐握者终其身畦复畦之不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319375_comment'></div>虽天雨，犹有憾也，若乘雨之云，负月之露，以出乎圹埌之野，则青青陵陂，累累古冶，吾庸知其初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319375_comment'></div>芊绵者春也，采采者人也，大以畦大，小以畦小，亦无人焉而不我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319375_comment'></div>彼以无我为无畦者，正累我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319375_comment'></div>我则异于是，无我无不我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319375_comment'></div>王佐名铉，天资近道，学焉问焉，非无志于用者，吾故扩而辟之，可以观世，可以处世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319375_comment'></div>吾须溪农也，第五十八雨水中华山书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1319375_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1319289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大梵寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319289")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319289'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319289'>异时游豫章者必问秋屏列岫，意其广大观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319289_comment'></div>然出新城，道衢巷如城中，又四五里而倦，而后得三门敞然于民居鳞鳞间者，大梵寺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319289_comment'></div>乃周遭殿廊，不见所谓秋屏列岫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319289_comment'></div>已而入于僧房，则秋屏黯然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319289_comment'></div>小窗栏楯容数客止，而西山在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319289_comment'></div>忽焉如登丘出于屋极，又如幻维摩臂取诸江外，何其苍然几案间也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319289_comment'></div>于是徘徊徙倚，转而得列岫于天宁铁普贤之侧，诵山谷二甥、四灵紫芝之作者，未尝不喜而赋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319289_comment'></div>承平内地湖山千里，钟鸣鼓应，刹刹如如，岂知世有清野哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319289_comment'></div>一日戎衣起，登城楼，治蔺石渠荅，城下环万数千鳞鳞者必不使遗一甓，而屏、岫与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319289_comment'></div>盖自盛唐以来，四百馀年之迹灭，向之铁者收为流金人，亦何所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319289_comment'></div>然开关之日，兵如合符，晏不易肆，斯人仰栋俯寝，左江右湖如昨，而大梵丘墟不可复识矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319289_comment'></div>寺僧飘飖，客栖久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319289_comment'></div>东湖谢墅者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319289_comment'></div>宝祐相君渎山惠国之手筑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319289_comment'></div>规制邃严，高下横斜，仿昭文第，而丽都一城胜处，望环瀛藐仙集焉，何尘埃踽踽之所敢望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319289_comment'></div>至是无人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319289_comment'></div>其间马粪荒凉，病者居之，其名为安乐堂，瓠落大方，草树寒烟，林燕悽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319289_comment'></div>法印大师则大梵之一僧也，在谢公姻娅间如高屐道人，泛而言于公孙曰：「前钦翘，后马厩，可化马厩为梵宫，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319289_comment'></div>府判某曰：「噫，吾志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319289_comment'></div>总管某曰：「噫，公志也，犹半山公志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319289_comment'></div>厥既得请，则白之执政当涂，下至史胥徒，可者半；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319289_comment'></div>又白之军司马走马，则谁曰不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319289_comment'></div>盖茫如垂橐而归者累月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319289_comment'></div>一夕印梦神人纳之，旦而告李公如梦曰：「果然妙圣寿山也，奈何其敢弗力」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319289_comment'></div>如是又数月，病者去，馀者徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319289_comment'></div>岁丁丑月正元日，新大梵揭焉，皇皇日于其垣墉之不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319289_comment'></div>明年，修法堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319289_comment'></div>又明年扶楼阁，僧官间之毁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319289_comment'></div>又一二年，溯而得武宁周府于庐陵，为之起殿若门如制，是为耐轩公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319289_comment'></div>自是庄严诸好，集施少多，而其徒亦各自竭，唯印最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319289_comment'></div>盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319289_comment'></div>金碧辉辉，如第新成，又为诸方最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319289_comment'></div>既告成，己丑求文为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319289_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319289_comment'></div>世道亦多态已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319289_comment'></div>东湖者吾不知其初，由开辟以来，章亥之所步，神禹之所经营，孰非夫佛之所谓清净法身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319289_comment'></div>是湖也，曾不当礨孔之一，其鞠为民蔬不知几何年，而化为高明，闭为窈窕，东湖不与知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319289_comment'></div>书生辛勤建立，传子又孙，而反乎复者，飘茵堕溷，至使人指公塾而叹，而公塾不与知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319289_comment'></div>佛之为道，至是有可言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319289_comment'></div>今其颓垣断础岁修岁异，复如王侯邸第，以此易彼，更比于昔之秋屏者而胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319289_comment'></div>回视同时故家陈迹，有愿为如此而不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319289_comment'></div>人以为游观春服之始，而不知太空变幻，乃且从坏得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319289_comment'></div>方其颡驹瘴卒，呻吟满目，呕泄污秽，有肯顾而有之者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319289_comment'></div>物莫垢于此矣，人亦何用存垢净于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319289_comment'></div>今之所成未有非坏也，使其不寂，是坏者犹在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319289_comment'></div>夫必坏而后归于寂，寂亦坏也，而自是无坏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1319289_comment'></div>吾以坏观色，以色观世，而知佛身之所以存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1319289_comment'></div>彼吊其所亡，而又幸其不终废者，未必非达道者之所悯然笑，而骚人羁客犹区区过是而不释也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1319289_comment'></div>呜呼，其真以为理乱有关于天地与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1319289_comment'></div>印号可山，能赋，地大心劳，出于其力者十七八，吾儒能事有不能及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1319289_comment'></div>顾眷焉慊焉，托于言语文字以久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1319289_comment'></div>虽然，数世之后，赋东湖者苍苔夕照，得吾文读之，犹如西山笑堕泪，方悟昔之秋屏者徒以绮语习业系人心如此，亦不得不怃然失也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1319289_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年9月</a>　元蒙丞相莽哈代出镇江西，四十余天亡，九月葬，为之作祭文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　居家庐陵读书，江万里外甥刘复村来访。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年</a>　居家庐陵，乡贤朱墨轩八十，有贺词。作品：《临江仙》（旧日诗肠论斗酒）<span class='inlineComment2'>（词作系年据吴熊和等《唐宋词汇评·两宋卷》第3737页。）</span><div id='poem_91101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91101?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>贺默轩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1291年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91101")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91101'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91101'>旧日诗肠论斗酒，风流怀抱如倾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91101'>几年不听渭城声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91101'>尊前无贺老，卷里少弥明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91101'>闻说语言都好，便应步履全轻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91101'>长生第一是风僧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91101'>额前书八十，能说又能行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_91101_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年</a>　本年为乡贤王槐城六十一岁寿作贺词。作品：《沁园春》（六十一翁）<div id='poem_91041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>和槐城自寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91041")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91041'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91041'>六十一翁，垂银带鱼，插四角轮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91041'>把百个今朝，重排花甲，十年前事，似臼齑辛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91041'>骰选功名，酒中富贵，管取当筵满劝旬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91041'>槐知道，待二郎做甚，父子封申。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91041_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91041'>便应际会昌辰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91041'>怕林下相逢未是真。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91041'>看焚芰裂荷，起钟山笑，卖田僦马，堕贡生贫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91041'>后六十年，有无穷事，是宰官身是报身。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91041_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91041'>年来好，莫做他宰相，便是全人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_91041_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年</a>　本年春，为前年卒于江西的莽哈代作美棠文。作品：《丞相莽哈代美棠碑文》<div id='poem_1319400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丞相莽哈岱美棠碑文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319400")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319400'>至元二十七年秋九月，丞相莽哈岱以江西省治庐陵，凡四十日薨于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319400_comment'></div>又二日丧行，居民望过车，罢市长恸，至不可忍闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319400_comment'></div>阖城士大夫哭于野者不约而集，无不相向而吊，依依憔悴无聊之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319400_comment'></div>田野闻之，惊顿踊绝，至有负贩之人不自知弃其所求，望庐垂涕而返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319400_comment'></div>既数月，有自北方来者号于马上，儿童父老闻其声者，喟然而哀痛之如新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319400_comment'></div>今期年矣，省还迹远，燧改情迁，而语及当日，犹为之饮泣而悲，哽咽而叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319400_comment'></div>方公之未至也，揭竿满野，环赣及汀历历无墟烟，吾郊关之御夺者，混相浊如市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319400_comment'></div>公之来也，悄乎其容，肃然而无声，不惟贪夫股战，军伍旗帜改观，而盗贼望风褫魄，凛焉以消者，复不知其几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319400_comment'></div>不惟城无嚣尘，里无夜惊，而昔之门扃户棘者蛰见天日熙然其如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319400_comment'></div>不惟长亭短堠行歌逆旅，而深山长谷妇人孺子与荷戈之士杂踵，而无何，近邑近州，行者达曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319400_comment'></div>皆旷十数年所未见，虽太平全盛，不过如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319400_comment'></div>或谓公之在事四十日止耳，即四十日间，有所诛罚耸动，亦何能家至户到？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319400_comment'></div>未尝按一贪吏也，又未尝杀一无道也，而民之畏之爱之，如将见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319400_comment'></div>赤眉、黄巾之不可胜殄，虽血之于此，犹惧其复生于彼，从古然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319400_comment'></div>乃不待草芟兽狝，不用三令五申，不必形格势禁，而威信之如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319400_comment'></div>民之思斁，朝暮四三，使公犹存，饥食渴饮，政未必人人而济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319400_comment'></div>前乎公者有矣，后乎公者亦未必不尤贤于公也，而推论斯人有一日生聚之安，若浮若沉以至今，此譬诸荒垦，实自公始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319400_comment'></div>独吾侪小人窃欲求公之所以致此者而不可得也，或者其福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319400_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319400_comment'></div>余读坡公所为《温国文正公碑》，中言「何自知之，何自知之」，极古人词辩反覆形容之盛，徵今日之事，则亦不以为过耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319400_comment'></div>所谓立之斯立，道之斯行，绥之斯来，动之斯和，非七日司寇见之行事，虽夫子犹疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319400_comment'></div>因是使人思前史，区区必有不尽得于言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319400_comment'></div>余以忧患馀生，延喘民间，亲见《甘棠》《角弓》之诵，欲备言其美则不可尽，欲参论其事乃无一有，盖矫然为之踌躇远想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319400_comment'></div>若尹长安之桓东虎穴，朱子元之奋髯抵几，李临淮之斩将立威，此人皆疾声厉色以胜之，仅济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319400_comment'></div>公于斯民有百年之爱，而无一日之功，虽善论者莫能述也，兹非古之君子不言而信，不怒而民威于鈇钺者与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319400_comment'></div>柳子厚谓吕衡州之死，哭之者逾月，哀声交于北南，舟船之上下必呱呱然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319400_comment'></div>又有谓化光何以得此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319400_comment'></div>以今揆昔，容复过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319400_comment'></div>哭死而哀，非为生者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319400_comment'></div>我观九京而誉武子，百世而下，故当识其何心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319400_comment'></div>晋人望羊叔子之碑而堕泪，则叔子自为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319400_comment'></div>公之没也，若士若民请于省府祠之，省曰「吾责也」，府亦曰「吾责也」，其门生故吏则又曰「吾责也」，民士因不敢为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319400_comment'></div>至二十九年春复请，府经历济南孙某以其俸独倡成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319400_comment'></div>孙盖公所辟以自辅者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319400_comment'></div>民士共高其谊，曰：「我则何力于斯」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319400_comment'></div>则相与植碑于学，以其诗来请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319400_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319400_comment'></div>后之人有读是碑而不堕泪者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319400_comment'></div>余亦何足以发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319400_comment'></div>系之以诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1319400'>衮衣绣斧，来旬来抚，里门昼开，官路夜旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319400_comment'></div>绣斧衮衣，今以丧归，寘予中道，卒误畴依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319400_comment'></div>悠悠行舟，惨惨四野，亡羊不知，狭路悲哑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319400_comment'></div>鼎饕释惧，林啸伏兴，山哀浦思，虎逝龙升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319400_comment'></div>蜀怀孔明，寒食祭路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319400_comment'></div>魏感梁公，聚哭碑下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319400_comment'></div>谁欤祠者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1319400_comment'></div>公有门生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1319400_comment'></div>我往营之，众志乃平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1319400_comment'></div>甘棠憩只，杕杜逝只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1319400_comment'></div>峨峨此碑，亦堕泪只！</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1319400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年</a>　为去年建成的长沙廉坊司题名作记。作品：《长沙廉访司题名记》<div id='poem_1319301' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319301' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319301?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长沙廉访司题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319301")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319301_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319301'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319301'>春正月而岁新，人情改饰脩洁，必无肯复仍其旧者，重天道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319301_comment'></div>故湖南肃政廉访司之题名始此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319301_comment'></div>肃政廉访司者，至元二十有八年以按察司玩废，更其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319301_comment'></div>首选当世人望有风力者为之，观听竦然，如霆行空，必将有所涤荡震厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319301_comment'></div>至之日，列城肃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319301_comment'></div>湖南带岭峤，隔江汉，地大去天远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319301_comment'></div>地大故难治，去天远故不尽闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319301_comment'></div>今其民安俗便，不待愬而救，贪夫远利知耻，虽欲假一二以徇，而厥罪无繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319301_comment'></div>又如秋之为令，行于草木，已而惟见天高而气清，潦雾俱尽，自亦不知其所以然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319301_comment'></div>于是廉司之建逾年矣，伻求文于庐陵以为之记，重新制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319301_comment'></div>按《春秋》未笔削前，楚有《梼杌》，专记人之恶，夫子以《春秋》易之，而义主于秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319301_comment'></div>湖南故楚，贪吏之昔也如杌，而诸君子之肃也亦如夫子之为秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319301_comment'></div>恭惟圣天子之命则有辞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319301_comment'></div>且按察犹廉访也，而必易之，宁惟易之，而肇揆之曰「肃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319301_comment'></div>如加冠弥尊，岂贵名哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319301_comment'></div>顾諟之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319301_comment'></div>按察者日求人之过，而肃政者先正己而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319301_comment'></div>汉万石君家不言而令行，小不释意，子弟至无所容措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319301_comment'></div>况立乎百官庶民之上，不见其形视其影，所谓不怒而民威于鈇钺者，岂可以旦暮致哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319301_comment'></div>意必有出于击断斩伐之外矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319301_comment'></div>方诸君子之来也，湖南之人相与闻而喜曰：是尝为某官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319301_comment'></div>在事之诸贤又必有闻而兴者曰：是尝以玉雪称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319301_comment'></div>则亦不待褰帷正色、揽辔扬声，而不仁者远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319301_comment'></div>此其想见风采隐然在题名之先者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319301_comment'></div>他日之奏事而归也，都人士聚而观者不又曰：是尝为湖南廉访者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319301_comment'></div>夫使天下移风易俗，回心而乡道者，其在斯人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319301_comment'></div>其在斯人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319301_comment'></div>此其属餍厚望，蔼然在题名之后者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319301_comment'></div>吾江西人也，昔者得之徐公子方焉，曰：是尝为湖南按察者，是尝为湖南按察而肃者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319301_comment'></div>是碑之立，锵然与子方前后联裾叠佩，鸣玉相应，不知其亦万一有能为江西来者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319301_comment'></div>独后我乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319301_comment'></div>盖愿言不获，如见其人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1319301_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年</a>　春，应友人邀请作龟山书院记。作品：《南剑龟山书院记》<div id='poem_1319286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南剑龟山书院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1293年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319286")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319286'>建炎中，寇毁将乐，独题杨文靖公之门曰：「此龟山先生屋，不可焚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319286_comment'></div>由是宅故在，为祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319286_comment'></div>复斋陈公宓守剑，又即祠为书院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319286_comment'></div>至元三十年春，蜀某府判以郡督至县，求先生之庐拜焉，则燬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319286_comment'></div>燬又五年矣，徬徨得故基草间，捐俸锄修，邑士慨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319286_comment'></div>适溪涨木刊，来中梁柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319286_comment'></div>不半月堂成，乃白总府台省为书院如旧，殿门祭器踵就，以记请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319286_comment'></div>或疑先生当不可为之时，为世麟止，而胡文定公谓其时能用，犹半可救，安在其为半也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319286_comment'></div>余曰：噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319286_comment'></div>士以处为高，不知圣贤之皇皇也，岂以一身重于天下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319286_comment'></div>当其际会，亦岂谓家国之事直由一书生反手为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319286_comment'></div>任有大小，大任可为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319286_comment'></div>求之吾君而非其任焉，求之吾相而非其任焉，如知其不可而为之，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319286_comment'></div>畏天命也，吾能为其半而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319286_comment'></div>古所谓以身为时者，未有非其半也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319286_comment'></div>自非险倾战国之士，安能使尽变其素而惟吾所欲为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319286_comment'></div>春秋者天道之半也，譬犹寒也以暑易之，几何其不为异物也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319286_comment'></div>夫所谓绥来动和者，类非后人力量之所能也，惟立乎人之本，朝而歌者之田止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319286_comment'></div>不幸而与小人比，染鼎者如有所惮而不敢发，放麑者亦往往有其意焉，而世道之可为者从是兆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319286_comment'></div>此则先生之所能为也，所谓半也非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319286_comment'></div>且先生尝议六馆矣，独请择祭酒德望以靖诸生而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319286_comment'></div>甚哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319286_comment'></div>文定公之论，为自有见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319286_comment'></div>党锢之诸贤欲以一日为平生而不能半，元祐之经筵又欲以一身为千古而过其半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319286_comment'></div>龟山远矣，后人尊之，其必有以信夫文定之论，而龟山之道为不废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319286_comment'></div>抑吾因是而重有感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319286_comment'></div>自古德行之士，朝廷不知也，州里不知也，而盗贼小人尝知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319286_comment'></div>物论之不齐久矣，此不齐而彼齐何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319286_comment'></div>鼎也，追蠡也，亦魑魅者畏之耳，人乃以为玩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319286_comment'></div>异哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319286_comment'></div>斯文之绝续则有命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319286_comment'></div>河畀洛陈，而书院复起，此世道之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319286_comment'></div>虽然，微今之役，则君子之泽如可已也，岂不悲哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319286_comment'></div>凡循旧易，继绝难，是间虽小，其有功于杞宋文献盖甚大，又非如涂涂附者也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1319286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年</a>　本年春日，有词记之。作品：《水调歌头》（又非他今年晴少）<div id='poem_91201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>甲午送春</a><span class='authorDate'>（1294年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91201")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91201'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91201'>春怜我。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91201'>我又自、怜伊不见侬赓和。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91201'>已无可奈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91201'>但愁满清漳，君归何处，无泪与君堕。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91201_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91201'>春去也，尚欲留春<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_91201", 91201, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>可可</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91201'>问公一醉能颇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91201'>钟情剩有词千首，待写大招招些。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91201'>休阿那。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91201'>阿那看、荒荒得似江南么。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91201_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年5月5日</a>　端午节和邓剡有唱和。作品：《摸鱼儿》（醒复醒、行吟泽畔）<div id='poem_91213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91213'>魂归否。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91213'>记昔与诸贤，共谈洛下，曾识老人父。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91213_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91213'>牛衣泪，冷落闻鸡东府。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91213'>风尘曾独深虑。<div showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91212?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91212_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_91212'>今岁海棠迟开半月，然一夕如雪，无饮余者，赋此寄恨。</div><div id='poem_preface_91212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91212'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91212'>是他家、绛唇翠袖，可容卿有功否。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91212'>相思不到胭脂井，只隔东林烟柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91212'>春去又。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91212'>漫一夜东风，吹得花成旧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
