id='poem_sentence_5_91212_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91212'>人间事，大半归谋诸妇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91212'>不如意十八九。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91212'>敲门夜半窥园李，赤脚玉川惊走。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91212'>何处有。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91212'>笑旧日园林，佺巢蜀锦，处处可携手。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91212_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91216?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91216'>柳摇首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91216'>问溪上儿童，颇曾见我，有此故人否。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91216_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91216'>相逢地，还忆今宵三韭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91216'>青山知了迎候。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91216'>东风自送归帆去，吹得乱红沾袖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91216'>暮云皱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91216'>听杜宇高高，啼向无何有。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91216'>江花垂手。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91216'>任春色重来，江花更好，难可少年又。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91216_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91215' class='poemTitle id='poem_title_91215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91215'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91215'>待欲归、家山未得，方知名不如酒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91215'>丹砂便做金勾漏，难遣鬓青似柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91215'>试搔首。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91215'>记移竹南塘，又是三年后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91215'>情怀非旧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91215'>渊明中路相候。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91215'>便持当金貂，赊取邻家有。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91215'>小儿拍手。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91215'>笑昨醉如泥，盟言止酒，何事醒来又。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91215_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91208?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91208'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91208'>醉与君、狂歌又笑，不知当日何调。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91208'>孤山梅下吟魂冷，说甚那时苏小。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91208'>沧波眇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91208'>奈此岛，累累竟是谁家表。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91208'>归欤白鸟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91208'>看四圣飘香，朱门金榜，化作竺飞峤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91208_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91208'>衰也久，旧游梦翠禽绕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91208'>坱兮轧、皎兮窈。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91208'>相思一夜窗前白，谁识余怀渺渺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91208'>残年了。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91208'>听画角，悲凉又是霜天晓。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91208'>馀音杳缈。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91208'>叹五十之年，我加八九，君隔几科诏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91208_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年9月9日</a>　重阳节，和友人登高，有词赋之。词序曰：“甲午九日牛山作”作品：《减字木兰花》（旧游山路）《水调歌头》（不饮强须饮）<div id='poem_91163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91163?labeling=true' target='_blank'>减字木兰花<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>甲午九日午山作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1294年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91163")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91163'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91163'>旧游山路。落在秋阴最深处。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91163'>风雨重阳。无蝶无花更断肠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91163_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91163'>天知老矣。莫累门生与儿子。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91163'>不用登高。高处风吹帽不牢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91163'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_91163_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1295&endYear=1295')">1295年4月</a>　友人陈俞卒多年，为之撰写墓志铭。作品：《陈礼部墓志铭》<div id='poem_1319405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈礼部墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1295年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319405")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319405'>宝祐丙辰之策士也，既日昃，再驾临轩，有少年首上对，彻亲览，卷首有「临御以来，如日正中」语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319405_comment'></div>及唱第，进呈次第七，上手擢易首，唱第七，既又不满，寘首，唱第四，第四则三山陈俞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319405_comment'></div>于是宝庆三十又三年矣，特讳言久，前别院命赋题「久于道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319405_comment'></div>以忤闻，故草茅附会如再中，然前彻览，后易寘，皆命也，而俞策亦实有及霅丘者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319405_comment'></div>舜卿尝语余：「考官不能使俞第一，天子不能使俞第七」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319405_comment'></div>其自信无怨如此，而亦从是退飞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319405_comment'></div>初君授静江军节度推官，开庆与吉州推两易，故君以己未东至庐陵办守御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319405_comment'></div>明年江上清，军閒，得余诗于它许，疑不属，余为举子美「丸药流莺啭」，君瞿然曰：「是在俞术中而不悟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319405_comment'></div>自是莫逆于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319405_comment'></div>每坐尚友斋，倚梧竹，极谈世事成坏，即使长急召不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319405_comment'></div>幕辨粲然，无所回屈，其辞可著为令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319405_comment'></div>李肯斋芾健吏事，称不及不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319405_comment'></div>去之日，有《誓心录》三卷，取欧公夷陵语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319405_comment'></div>人生至今德之，而媢者谤者为不少矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319405_comment'></div>有以科斗竹书献当国者，喜且惊曰：「彼白屋安得此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319405_comment'></div>必平园公家物也，讵止此」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319405_comment'></div>献者惧，诡曰：「我出陈推官后矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319405_comment'></div>语由是喧，不辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319405_comment'></div>迟岁年，得监库，稍迁太学录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319405_comment'></div>咸淳除博士，竟坐前语逐，不辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319405_comment'></div>它日《谢丞相启》云：「人之云云，谓盗周公之宝玉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319405_comment'></div>萧然坦迤，玩世无闷如此，而亦从是老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319405_comment'></div>又四年而差充福建帅干阙，至此乡嫌，改添差不釐务，久之又改添差福建运干待次，于是咸淳八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319405_comment'></div>复除太博，十月免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319405_comment'></div>乃德祐前予湖州别驾，德祐改建宁，于是国事非矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319405_comment'></div>肯斋李公之为湖南也，强起君，君亦浩然以身许之，会文丞相脱身渡淮，归行都建督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319405_comment'></div>景炎以大著除君督机，君请据汀摇赣，出江西毋缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319405_comment'></div>君本赴湖南，至是哭湖南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319405_comment'></div>岁尽以所部福安军发谷口，道病，至汀卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319405_comment'></div>有赵同舍文自君归，能言巷居人梦绛纱笼甚盛，迎陈礼部去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319405_comment'></div>旦果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319405_comment'></div>文公哭之恸，葬伏虎山，题曰「草亭先生之墓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319405_comment'></div>君年二十九出文榜，至是四十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319405_comment'></div>又明年文公北日，门人林达可始以行状来请铭，则君死十九年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319405_comment'></div>其言正羽檄徵兵时，居萧夫人忧，苫块寱语于用武之无地，最后作《苍雪林辞》二叠，不可忍闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319405_comment'></div>李公期君以管葛之事，君亦赞文公以张李之功，其反覆策军事，谋家基，语如史，验如卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319405_comment'></div>当未行，梦丞相予黑笔，视黑籍如军书，少焉登一舟，若之贬所，风月凄冷，殆非人世境也，「吾死已夫」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319405_comment'></div>亲友共留其行，不可，曰：「士为知己死，苟利社稷何恨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319405_comment'></div>吾登草亭望风雨，欲一人共死不可得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319405_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319405_comment'></div>我知舜卿，使朝坐燕与，谊肯弃老母弱子，遁荒在人间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319405_comment'></div>星言赴难，缟素为资，得君军师，尚不甚败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319405_comment'></div>「临河救溺，不卜命之短长」，每诵郭元瑜此语，悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319405_comment'></div>其乘飞至屋，天也，伤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319405_comment'></div>吾友生不得志于前，死无知己于后，其心之所乐直文字耳，而文史亦绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319405_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1319405_comment'></div>吾欲观乎九京也，其有恨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1319405_comment'></div>无恨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1319405_comment'></div>以君自言其死为不恨，则知如余者不死而恨也，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1319405_comment'></div>景定末，余留建，君留京，君画二龙寄余，题曰甲子上元日，并赞，每展诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1319405_comment'></div>后死何为，吾所知所厚，离合何限，求仙才与灵气惟舜卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1319405_comment'></div>古心江公尝荐君馆职，不合，黄华甫国云：「台中日月论，公客添一客耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1319405_comment'></div>十五年间，夷溷蹠廉，衣冠道尽，君不惟少合，亦少可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1319405_comment'></div>閒居日长，夺虎豅，起草亭，俯晴晦，其在下种梅数百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1319405_comment'></div>长歌入云，俗子无足还顾，颓然自爱，韵度乃出苏子美上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1319405_comment'></div>为文达大家数，四六尤高宕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1319405_comment'></div>诗本荆公，而每见每进，虽在怨诽，有柳州、南涧之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1319405_comment'></div>初学六一公帖，卒自为体，如閒花异草，风日清美，皆余所不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1319405_comment'></div>尝手写《楞严》、《圆觉》、《金刚》三经，去庐陵日弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1319405_comment'></div>先死七年，葬其妻郑氏般若山，面草亭，中为寿藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1319405_comment'></div>君死子弱，不克归葬，每岁寒食，驰仆裹饭，洒伏虎丘而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1319405_comment'></div>既十五年辛卯，乃启而合诸郑宜人之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1319405_comment'></div>陈氏长乐，世次见石室翁碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1319405_comment'></div>二子：玚、环，环为族父企后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1319405_comment'></div>君兄会、弟龠皆同舍，会先二年卒，龠后六年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1319405_comment'></div>玚谋铭于达可，达可曰：「有先生之友会孟，顾道远日迫，请刻之墓上其可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1319405_comment'></div>由是林君之请勤矣，林君之谊高矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1319405_comment'></div>吾铭成，则葬后之五年乙未四月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1319405_comment'></div>君著述多，圹志传之矣，此不载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1319405_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1319405'>长歌兮莽苍，青松关兮白玉堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1319405_comment'></div>奄尘昏兮夕阳，我不起兮不如彼童汪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1319405_comment'></div>君墨缞兮何壮，操余彗兮彗霣光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1319405_comment'></div>忽反顾兮魁沦降，君不归兮犹葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1319405_comment'></div>湖山兮朝行，兰萎蕙绝兮谄子浪浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1319405_comment'></div>信终古兮谁芳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1319405_comment'></div>君余铭兮宰上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1319405_comment'></div>余麟兮不祥，行伥伥兮不得四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1319405_comment'></div>蹇思君兮天望，君为龙兮奚伤！</div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1319405_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='be568445214c48e9840567d34d64f8ac_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("be568445214c48e9840567d34d64f8ac");'><span id='be568445214c48e9840567d34d64f8ac_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1297')">1296-1297年</a>，65-66岁</div><div id='be568445214c48e9840567d34d64f8ac' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年8月15日</a>　中秋节有词贺，题作“丙申中秋”作品：《唐多令》（明月满河洲）<div id='poem_91130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91130?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐多令<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>丙申中秋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1296年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91130")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91130'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91130'>明月满河洲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91130'>星河带月流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91130'>料素娥、独倚琼楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91130'>竟是何年何药误，魂梦冷、不禁秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91130_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91130'>少日梦龙头。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91130'>知君犹梦不。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91130'>算虚名、不了闲愁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91130'>便有鹄袍三万辈，应不是、旧京游。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_91130_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年8月16日</a>　节后第二日又有词，序云：“丙申中秋两道人出示四十年前濯缨楼赏月水调，……明日又续之。”作品：《水调歌头》（此夕酹江月）<div id='poem_90977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_90977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/90977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>丙申中秋，两道人出示四十年前濯缨楼赏月水调。臞仙和，意已尽，明日又续之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1296年8月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_90977")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_90977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_90977'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_90977'>此夕酹江月，犹记濯缨秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_90977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_90977'>濯缨又去如水，安得主人留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_90977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_90977'>旧日登楼长笑，此日新亭对泣，秃鬓冷飕飕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_90977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_90977'>木落下极浦，渔唱发中洲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_90977_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_90977'>芙蓉阙，鸳鸯阁，凤凰楼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_90977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_90977'>夜深白露纷下，谁见湿萤流。<div id='poem_sentence_5_90977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_90977'>自有此生有客，但恨有鱼无酒，不了一生浮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_90977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_90977'>重省看潮去，今夕是杭州。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_90977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年</a>　本年冬，为庐陵县学立心堂作记。作品：《庐陵县学立心堂记》<div id='poem_1319349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐陵县学立心堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1296年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319349")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319349'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319349'>余年十三，以童子试县学堂上，后十年而进士第一者亦于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319349_comment'></div>噫，其如梦耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319349_comment'></div>当其时，堂跂跂集，不可一布武，讲于斯，食于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319349_comment'></div>后偪县丞簿廨，邻嚣爨其左，喑分寸不得入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319349_comment'></div>每霖溢，沟浸无可泄，亦百年于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319349_comment'></div>盛时美宰圜顾无策，仅疏为楼窗数尺，飞雨沾扅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319349_comment'></div>比年邑改是，赘旒者尚不废坠，而教谕鼎来，廪空而客去，况有能议改拓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319349_comment'></div>迨萧涣可至，独慊然陋已，起而图之，则向之丞簿廨莽焉已久，屡请僦回，复岁馀而后下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319349_comment'></div>沟埒馀五丈，厥既荒度，而老兵居之，僦之不可，栖之左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319349_comment'></div>已而废寺炽然，有禅居僧赝契齿而胁，新安学田将夺，涣可指学碑辨，危而后定，而工役亦少间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319349_comment'></div>兴造未易为也，难又若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319349_comment'></div>吏且接踵，而向之役既而不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319349_comment'></div>斯堂比进士第一高深倍广称，盖凿而筑之三尺，翼以雨窗，然后席函丈馀，然后池雨四集，然后取楼窗西之为藏书，易米廪为小学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319349_comment'></div>观者环回，不独棂星之新其外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319349_comment'></div>涣可曰：「吾为乡校，不可以累后人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319349_comment'></div>以己力任其费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319349_comment'></div>惟是棂星、小学等成，终而会，涣可复以其奉廪不足，诸生感曰：「此悃悃复为谁事」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319349_comment'></div>请各效供奉，馀足焉，由是不毫发挂簿责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319349_comment'></div>有赞有叹，无敢间起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319349_comment'></div>丙申冬终，求堂名，予命之「立心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319349_comment'></div>是日也，揖诸生而进之曰：学何为也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319349_comment'></div>政尔不为，抑复谁能彊此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319349_comment'></div>自有天地而斯人立焉，斯人天地心也，其心天地者学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319349_comment'></div>伏羲尧舜氏作，而后人得其所以为人者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319349_comment'></div>伏羲尧舜氏不作，而立焉者私淑于曲阜之匹夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319349_comment'></div>自曲阜千年，而天下为学校之天下，以至今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319349_comment'></div>邑无小，曲阜是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319349_comment'></div>学无小，伏羲尧舜氏是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319349_comment'></div>洪水汩陈，三光五岳之不得其宁，禹以胼胝为平成功，当是时也，天地托之禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319349_comment'></div>师尚父之所经营，父师微启之所归往，而独首阳之子戚然其间，为纲为常，当是时也，天地托之夷、齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319349_comment'></div>春秋者山林诛讨为尤难，于一圣二贤而接乎伏羲尧舜氏，以垂万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319349_comment'></div>然微言绝而邪说塞，孟轲氏以闻知辟之，廓如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319349_comment'></div>当是时也，天地托之孔孟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319349_comment'></div>俎豆之，弦歌之，虽存乎寥廓，而天下以学不学为治乱，人亦未尝不以不学为其耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319349_comment'></div>向非隐然者检而律之，则游梁而困者皆为仪、秦，读城旦书者皆为鞅、斯，封君侯王皆为五霸，而功利与刑名交骛于世，民之黔赭其不鬼魅几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319349_comment'></div>党锢清流虽无益于存亡之数，然此风不竞，将宦寺小人皆迭执其柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319349_comment'></div>斯人者虽不幸，乃其心则布之天下国家矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319349_comment'></div>故尝谓韩、欧当平世，崇辨拒邪又在关洛之先、杨墨之外，为学校功宗，皆所谓天地立心者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319349_comment'></div>夫庸人者不足以为天地心矣，异氏者不足以为天地心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319349_comment'></div>千载一时，科举废而学校兴，学校兴而人材出，故学校又为天地心之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319349_comment'></div>予也若昔堂下之童子也，丰碑在刊，忠节如前，盖荏苒衰迟，而有道德初心之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319349_comment'></div>故于斯堂也，始之喟然，终之喟然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319349_comment'></div>涣可名涣，时同官赵时第、前职周适道、朱介实相成之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1319349_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年</a>　庐陵先贤朱氏老人生日，有寿词，题曰：“寿朱氏老人七十三岁”作品：《金缕曲》（七十三年矣）<div id='poem_91071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金缕曲<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>寿朱氏老人七十三岁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1296年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91071")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91071'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91071'>七十三年矣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91071'>记小人、四百四十，五番甲子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91071'>看到蓬莱水清浅，休说树犹日如此。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91071'>但梦梦、昨非今是。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91071'>一曲尊前离鸾操，抚铜仙、清泪如铅水。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91071'>歌未断，我先醉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91071_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91071'>新来画得耆英似。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91071'>似灞桥、风雪吟肩，水仙梅弟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91071'>里巷依稀灵光在，飞过劫灰如洗。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91071'>笑少伴、乌衣馀几。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91071'>老子平生何曾默<span class='inlineComment2'>（号默轩）</span>，暮年诗、句句皆成史。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91071'>个亥字，甲申起。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_91071_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年</a>　本年冬，有客贾文广和樊君仲璋来拜谒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　谋葬江万里，奔走都昌。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b2f14c1f14584b07ac19ddff11e51aaa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b2f14c1f14584b07ac19ddff11e51aaa");'><span id='b2f14c1f14584b07ac19ddff11e51aaa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>，49岁</div><div id='b2f14c1f14584b07ac19ddff11e51aaa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>　探寻到江万里子江镐下落，再次北上都昌，谋葬江万里，为其石山庵定名归来庵。年底作归来庵记文。作品：《归来庵记》<div id='poem_1319342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>归来庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1280年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319342")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319342'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319342'>归来者，古心先生石山庵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319342_comment'></div>先生生于林塘，老于同野，苑于芝山之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319342_comment'></div>死而不死者在宇宙，不死而死者人心是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319342_comment'></div>嗟乎，归来乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319342_comment'></div>归来乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319342_comment'></div>四方上下其何归乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319342_comment'></div>昔者闻之大禹曰，死归也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319342_comment'></div>归有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319342_comment'></div>有战败而归者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319342_comment'></div>有去家愈远，丧其所挟而归者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319342_comment'></div>有呻吟中路，流离悔恨而不得归者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319342_comment'></div>有赴蹈不顾，毁伤其面目者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319342_comment'></div>有优游卒岁，全名于牖下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319342_comment'></div>归有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319342_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319342_comment'></div>人谓之不死奚益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319342_comment'></div>东坡谓延州来季子庶几不死，然终春秋之世，馀皇姑蔑之不返，甬东泰伯之不祀，复能萧然人间，若无意于去来者，则吾亦不知其何心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319342_comment'></div>盖不死而死者，人心是也，悲哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319342_comment'></div>是庵为先生之所手筑，意其魂魄犹不忘是间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319342_comment'></div>皋复之道于此乎，于彼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319342_comment'></div>未可知，乃作《山中归来之歌》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319342_comment'></div>作歌者谁，先生之门人宋玉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319342_comment'></div>歌曰：皋归来兮山之阳，高冠青云兮拥白露以为裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319342_comment'></div>遇子卿于盛汉兮，十九年而牧羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319342_comment'></div>天荒荒兮日星无光，地茫茫兮两乳雷琅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319342_comment'></div>箜篌哀兮湘瑟，御过平实兮玉堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319342_comment'></div>皋归来兮山之阴，而为阁兮宫沉沉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319342_comment'></div>清风时至兮芳草满林，山空无人兮猿啾啾而夜吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319342_comment'></div>父前而弟后兮熙春载临，忽相顾以流涕兮又痛哭而不可禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319342_comment'></div>彼紫芝之垂绝兮遗我哀音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319342_comment'></div>庵成于某年月日，记成于庚辰十二月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1319342_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
赣州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e49097f2d7404b5da9e82fc4c9328fbf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e49097f2d7404b5da9e82fc4c9328fbf");'><span id='e49097f2d7404b5da9e82fc4c9328fbf_link' id='poem_sentence_9_91226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91226'>听父老，歌襦裤。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
建瓯（建宁府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4d84cbcff4214a3f9591b399f4ba0fbc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4d84cbcff4214a3f9591b399f4ba0fbc");'><span id='4d84cbcff4214a3f9591b399f4ba0fbc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>，33岁</div><div id='4d84cbcff4214a3f9591b399f4ba0fbc' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>本年春，入江万里建宁幕府。作品：《摸鱼儿》（也何须、晴如那日）<span class='inlineComment2'>（词作系年据刘宗彬《刘辰翁年谱》第60页。）</span><div id='poem_91213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摸鱼儿<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91213")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91213_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91213'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91213'>三百年、人间天上，遽如许、遽如许。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91213'>落花寒食东风雨，漠漠长陵抔土。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91213'>魂归否。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91213'>怕些不分明，又堕人笺疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91213'>且无相负。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91213'>记昔与诸贤，共谈洛下，曾识老人父。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91213_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91213'>牛衣泪，冷落闻鸡东府。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91213'>风尘曾独深虑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91213'>子规声断长门晓，春梦不堪重做。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91213'>千万古。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91213'>但目极心伤，宛转虞兮楚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91213'>江东日暮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91213'>想野草荒田，而今何处，不待雍门鼓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91213_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91212' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91212' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91212?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91212_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_91212'>今岁海棠迟开半月，然一夕如雪，无饮余者，赋此寄恨。</div><div id='poem_preface_91212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91212'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91212'>是他家、绛唇翠袖，可容卿有功否。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91212'>相思不到胭脂井，只隔东林烟柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91212'>春去又。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91212'>漫一夜东风，吹得花成旧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91212'>无人举酒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91212'>但照影堤流，图他红泪，飘洒到襟袖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91212_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91212'>人间事，大半归谋诸妇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91212'>不如意十八九。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91212'>敲门夜半窥园李，赤脚玉川惊走。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91212_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91216?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_0_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91216'>中年怀抱萦萦处，看取伴烟和柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91216_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91215?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91215'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91215'>待欲归、家山未得，方知名不如酒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91215'>记移竹南塘，又是三年后。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91215_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91215'>种兰处，赢得青青种韭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91215'>渊明中路相候。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91215'>何须更待三三径，也自长拖衫袖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91215'>青袍皱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91215'>便持当金貂，赊取邻家有。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91215'>小儿拍手。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91215'>笑昨醉如泥，盟言止酒，何事醒来又。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91215_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_91208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91208?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91208'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91208'>醉与君、狂歌又笑，不知当日何调。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91208'>孤山梅下吟魂冷，说甚那时苏小。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91208'>沧波眇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91208'>奈此岛，累累竟是谁家表。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91208'>归欤白鸟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_91208'>看四圣飘香，朱门金榜，化作竺飞峤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_91208_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_91208'>衰也久，旧游梦翠禽绕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_91208'>坱兮轧、皎兮窈。<div id='poem_sentence_7_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_91208'>相思一夜窗前白，谁识余怀渺渺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_91208'>残年了。<div id='poem_sentence_9_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_91208'>听画角，悲凉又是霜天晓。<div id='poem_sentence_10_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_91208'>馀音杳缈。<div id='poem_sentence_11_91208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_91208'>叹五十之年，我加八九，君隔几科诏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_91208_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>初到建宁府，有词记录。作品：《水调歌头》（雨声深院里）<div id='poem_90986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_90986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/90986?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", id='poem_sentence_0_90986'>雨声深院里，歌扇小楼中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_90986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_90986'>当时飞燕马上，妖艳为谁容。<div id='poem_sentence_3_90986'>掠鬓过车骤，回首意冲冲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_90986_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_90986'>宝钗斜，云鬓乱，几曾逢。<div id='poem_sentence_4_90986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_90986'>谁知去三步远，此痛与君同。<div id='poem_sentence_5_90986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_90986'>玉箸残妆谁见，獭髓轻痕妙补，粉黛不须浓。<div id='poem_sentence_6_90986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_90986'>重见为低诉，馀恨更匆匆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_90986_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
吉水（吉州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='98a07e3dcefe4b859bdc6cd87da32cb3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("98a07e3dcefe4b859bdc6cd87da32cb3");'><span id='98a07e3dcefe4b859bdc6cd87da32cb3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1276')">1275-1276年</a>，44-45岁</div><div id='98a07e3dcefe4b859bdc6cd87da32cb3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年12月</a>　自永新转道至吉水虎溪避兵火。开始评点唐人诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年</a>　本年在吉水，曾游览名胜古迹。作品：《朝仙观记》<div id='poem_1319338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝仙观记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319338")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319338'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319338'>以香城山为南华，以南华为朝仙观，则自前吉州守天台叶丞相始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319338_comment'></div>华盖者北辰之宇也，山之穹然者象之，故为望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319338_comment'></div>今言华盖山者何其盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319338_comment'></div>初，临川郡有三峰云间，号江西高绝处，相传隐者浮丘公控鹤而上，顾尝约其弟子王若郭，后见于此，是为华盖山三仙翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319338_comment'></div>而所至高山必有二弟子之迹何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319338_comment'></div>盖昔者之皇皇其师也，于彼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319338_comment'></div>于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319338_comment'></div>未可知，故所在而见之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319338_comment'></div>繇临川溯永丰有西华山，又西至吉水东山为中华，繇中华上五十里得庐陵香城山，又高为南华，皆二弟子徘徊白云之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319338_comment'></div>而南华三峰略与华盖山相似，其下有忠简公胡氏居之，又庐陵望也，故南华最盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319338_comment'></div>余为记仙姓名，不求人知而知之者，曰浮丘公足矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319338_comment'></div>又求公之弟子而不可得，则曰是尝授诗申公，不乃与王子同耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319338_comment'></div>或曰，控鹤在老子前，与太子晋同时，其授诗亦犹老子二百馀岁见秦献公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319338_comment'></div>或曰，授诗后有王褒、王乔，皆《列仙传》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319338_comment'></div>殆是已，殆是已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319338_comment'></div>而郭又未见闻也，则曰王之郭也，变姓也，盖从兄弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319338_comment'></div>先后时代且不可知，而知其同姓从兄弟，变荒哉乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319338_comment'></div>方之外而不得，而方内败之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319338_comment'></div>某丘以地氏，氏浮丘者不一世，安在其为授诗翁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319338_comment'></div>且授诗翁荀卿门人，彼知授诗之为人师，而不知荀卿之于浮丘又其师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319338_comment'></div>仙籍多王氏，古今王乔六，聋俗肤引舛错无足證，而华盖山托为颜鲁公记如麻姑者尤俚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319338_comment'></div>华盖者北辰之宇也，山如华盖，可以出云致雨，斯望之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319338_comment'></div>浮丘先生，古之隐者也，隐始浮丘则仙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319338_comment'></div>自其弟子求之不可得，则隐矣，与之隐者不可知，为浮丘之役，则浮丘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319338_comment'></div>王与郭且不必问，而为乔、为褒、为子晋，譬千载之后，吾知香城之为南华耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319338_comment'></div>南华之为香城耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319338_comment'></div>于此有云，其下为雨，吾不知谁为之雨，则归之天，而天又谁为之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319338_comment'></div>意者其帝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319338_comment'></div>反而取诸裳衣衮冕焉，圭璧焉，耳目具而高明者，区区犹夫人焉，犹夫人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319338_comment'></div>今吾一举首而凛然临之，其明威，其明畏，其比人间南面，巍巍乎宫室之钜丽哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319338_comment'></div>羲皇尧舜氏，而天无称，虽有巫阳，莫之敢尸，而心之精神极其远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319338_comment'></div>想寥阳金阙，紫微玉皇，崇高富贵，备物典策，神而明之也，若此陋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319338_comment'></div>天无情，帝无形，仙无名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319338_comment'></div>以帝为主宰则人之也，无物者有物也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319338_comment'></div>以仙为某某则神之也，有物者犹无物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319338_comment'></div>仰而兹山兹仙也，犹仰而为天为帝也，其不可知也则亦至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319338_comment'></div>太山之上有巨人迹焉，曰昔黄帝战于此，闻者隐然笑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319338_comment'></div>及至山之有昆崙也，星之有牛女也，招焉指其过客，纪其时日，辨其处所，如所尝睹，如家人语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319338_comment'></div>古以至今山不崩，天不坠，厥亦若有持之者焉，而皆意之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319338_comment'></div>忧其崩且坠者为愚为诞，而知其所不可知者为智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319338_comment'></div>穷无穷，极无极，吾将證之南华，而南华老仙复隐然笑之，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319338_comment'></div>吾闻韩子之论山也，曰最远而独为宗，其神必灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319338_comment'></div>余避乱方山之下，天大雪，望香城雪，倚天照日，如峨嵋西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319338_comment'></div>其中峰高大，人指之曰朝仙观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319338_comment'></div>王玄洞其左，郭公岩其右，蝗旱祷焉，天灯出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319338_comment'></div>道士钟允升掌观事，与其师张次良焚修祝曰：惟宋万万年，子子孙孙惟王，永作神主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1319338_comment'></div>自有天地，不知何年此山为香城，香城生忠简，以匹夫捍城郭，以编修官按宰执，吾所知者其灵以此，其最盛以此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1319338_comment'></div>星沦岳踣，南北壅隔，近年始宗华盖，福华者无不在，则如忠简者尚有人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1319338_comment'></div>是为德祐元年，吉州南华山朝仙观记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1319338_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　暮春，离开吉水虎溪，前往庐陵永阳。其间有词文多篇。作品：《浣溪沙》（春日春风掠鬓须）<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》，第88-90页。）</span><div id='poem_91143' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_91143' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/91143?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浣溪沙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>虎溪春日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_91143")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_91143_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_91143'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_91143'>春日春风掠鬓须。<div id='poem_sentence_0_91143_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_91143'>乱山相对拥寒炉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_91143_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_91143'>彩鞭金胜一时无。<div id='poem_sentence_2_91143_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_91143'>自缕青丝成细柳，更堆残雪当凝酥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_91143_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_91143'>儿童且莫唱皇都。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_91143_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年2月</a>　避祸永阳。有文。作品：《虎溪莲社堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（避祸永阳，据李璞《刘辰翁三年行迹补考》第88-90页。）</span><div id='poem_1319339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虎溪莲社堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319339")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319339'>方山在青原东、东山西，泷江出其左右，村江其右，方山之泉出山下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319339_comment'></div>山束为峡，委蛇循峡，左右赴二江，是为虎溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319339_comment'></div>元年冬十二月，余避地虎溪，主萧氏，诸君幸哀我，馆且谷我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319339_comment'></div>余惟世方乱，蓬累而行，瓜牛以居，揭揭焉载其木主而无所可祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319339_comment'></div>一日步行田间，得精庐曰莲社，欣然蹶然，就而腊焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319339_comment'></div>社友十馀，中堂高洁，佛祖咸在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319339_comment'></div>道人觉就可晤语，请记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319339_comment'></div>余谓道人莲社本远公庐山，庐山前则亦虎溪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319339_comment'></div>远送客未尝过虎溪，谢灵运求入社不纳，而往来渊明，山水隐映，醉醒两相得，非以其徜徉方外，世味薄耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319339_comment'></div>渊明为参军六载，县八十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319339_comment'></div>余尘居寡谐，非无意斯世，名穆陵进士十又五年，独尝教授中都百六十日，罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319339_comment'></div>又三年，起从庐山公江东七阅月，从江东得掌故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319339_comment'></div>入修门四十五日，以忧归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319339_comment'></div>归又七年，而当德祐初元五月，召入馆，辞未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319339_comment'></div>十月除博士，道已阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319339_comment'></div>岁晚，自永新江转入虎溪，留虎溪三月矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319339_comment'></div>十年之间，仕已如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319339_comment'></div>去年庐山公以节死，谥文忠，惟余与同年萧献可皆公客，相对感念离合出处流落，惟师友之故，而余尤以贫似渊明，独诵其诗辞，百世下彷佛求一语不可得，以此愧恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319339_comment'></div>天其以余畸于彼而合于此，牵帅山水，至此逋播耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319339_comment'></div>何虎溪同，莲社同，道人相得又同志，为此堂记甲子，则余与渊明命也，亦本无高处，正自不得不尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319339_comment'></div>「八表同昏，平路伊阻」，诵《停云》此语，泪下露土，何能无情！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319339_comment'></div>此堂起咸淳二年，静观居士萧公某创为之，献可其弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319339_comment'></div>是年为德祐二年二月戊午社。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1319339_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d1a93597dd6d4dedbe0c18138e12228e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d1a93597dd6d4dedbe0c18138e12228e");'><span id='d1a93597dd6d4dedbe0c18138e12228e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年</a>，52岁</div><div id='d1a93597dd6d4dedbe0c18138e12228e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年8月15日</a>　中秋节在吉水与庐陵乡饮酒按察马德昌泛游江，有词。作品：《水调歌头》（群动各已息）<div id='poem_90993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_90993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/90993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>癸未中秋，吉文共马德昌泛江</a><span class='authorDate'>（1283年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_90993")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_90993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_90993'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_90993'>群动各已息，在汝梦中游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_90993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_90993'>尘埃大地如水，儿女不堪愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_90993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_90993'>寂寂古人安在，冉冉吾年如此，何处有高楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_90993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_90993'>客有洞箫者，泪下不能收。<div id='poem_sentence_3_90993_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_90993'>庾楼坠，秦楼渺，楚楼休。<div id='poem_sentence_4_90993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_90993'>知公所恨何事，不是为封侯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_90993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_90993'>自有此山此月，说甚何年何处，重泛木兰舟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_90993_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_90993'>起舞酹英魄，馀愤海西流。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_90993_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bbbf198fb974417581c88a57136dc90f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bbbf198fb974417581c88a57136dc90f");'><span id='bbbf198fb974417581c88a57136dc90f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年</a>，56岁</div><div id='bbbf198fb974417581c88a57136dc90f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年5月</a>　五月游吉水洞岩并作记。作品：《吉水洞岩朱陵观玉华坛记》<div id='poem_1319300' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319300' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319300?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吉水洞岩朱陵观玉华坛记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319300")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319300_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319300'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319300'>因泰山升中，于天近也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319300_comment'></div>地载神气而产五行，其尤高且大者，风雨之所交，云龙之所兴，仙圣之所往还，故柴望通，请雩切，登封极，陟配隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319300_comment'></div>况第为洞天三百六十之一，古之真人尝修炼于此，后之学者又冲举于此，则坛为饰焉，植圭璧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319300_comment'></div>其增高据胜，如东方明，如四郊合，岂直佳时远集，俯落帽以兴怀，迟暮同游，顾沈碑而横涕也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319300_comment'></div>洞岩在吾州南东吉水西，自贞元六年阎使君寀弃吉州锡名，遗荣隐兹山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319300_comment'></div>《唐会要》云，今岩石有若扉半阖、霤飞瀑者，相传入岩中石合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319300_comment'></div>繇使君前有谢仙，后有彭刘，又后有此山道童曾，俱无名，俱得道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319300_comment'></div>而南唐徐锴开宝初记称浮丘王郭尝游此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319300_comment'></div>道家《紫玄实录》遂称王郭洞为小华盖，指此古洞岩名实寿观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319300_comment'></div>治平改朱陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319300_comment'></div>涧水出东西两洞，入东洞，道古华盖阁，至瀑下，未至瀑数步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319300_comment'></div>径绝顶，迂回腾拿出瀑上，今为玉华坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319300_comment'></div>坛在曾仙童升处，夜有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319300_comment'></div>按江西惟抚州华盖山巢三仙，而吾州稍高山辄称华，如瑞华、佑华、南华者不一，惟中华盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319300_comment'></div>然稽其实，如上所记无一有，而洞岩自阎使君外不见称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319300_comment'></div>数方民之求福，草野勃兴，亦犹履巨迹而疑雨星，闻雊音而希陈宝，虽鸿濛之与语，而汗漫之与期，要皆不可致诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319300_comment'></div>然仙骥未归，隐然下记其处；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319300_comment'></div>虹光上烛，夜中犹际于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319300_comment'></div>则兹山之为玉华又近也，其不可诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319300_comment'></div>凡人间世质左契，彼凿空望走，此隐佚沈沦，则亦居其所者之有能不能也，而人物显晦犹是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319300_comment'></div>使众真杂遝者，非浮丘翁与其丹犹在是欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319300_comment'></div>吾尝挟二三子与父老争道，指山而问，在芗城五峰，忠简胡公在其下居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319300_comment'></div>永和清都，东坡、山谷游焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319300_comment'></div>佛塔其阴，钓台涓涓之所自出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319300_comment'></div>前望快阁，章贡横陈，想见安期老人自此而入海，周王南征，虫沙猿鹤之后先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319300_comment'></div>仙好楼居，楼莫尚于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319300_comment'></div>既下，道人请记，余笑曰：「宇宙兹山，谓自今日始可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319300_comment'></div>道人曰：「兹山宇宙，自今日耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319300_comment'></div>余谓二三子具笔墨，余为玉华记今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319300_comment'></div>自阎使君至今日四百九十二年，自宝寿观至今日三百三十一年，自朱陵至今日二百二十五年，自为玉华至今日乙丙丁二十有三月凡六百三十有三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319300_comment'></div>岁在娵訾，月旅蕤宾，丙丁统日，庚子御辰，余游山并记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1319300_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
彭泽（江州）

<div class='label1' id='a00bd8d2128843db988bad807290f91c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a00bd8d2128843db988bad807290f91c");'><span id='a00bd8d2128843db988bad807290f91c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>，49岁</div><div id='a00bd8d2128843db988bad807290f91c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>　年初与黄纯父相遇彭泽东湖。<br /></div>

-----title
峡江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f3d73fff763d4542a3728285e5763f34_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f3d73fff763d4542a3728285e5763f34");'><span id='f3d73fff763d4542a3728285e5763f34_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年</a>，54岁</div><div id='f3d73fff763d4542a3728285e5763f34' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年9月9日</a>　重阳节游玉笥山，有记文。作品：《玉笥山承天宫云堂记》<div id='poem_1319366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319366?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉笥山承天宫云堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(36803, "宋末元初", "刘辰翁", "poem_title_1319366")'>刘辰翁</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319366_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319366'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319366'>玉笥承天之云堂成，五星聚斗之岁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319366_comment'></div>先是，余游洞天，宿山房，见其成而去，为书「庐陵刘某过第一山」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319366_comment'></div>山中人求余记之，未暇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319366_comment'></div>其明年乙酉九日，登高把菊，望数峰如笥，意欣然记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319366_comment'></div>云者出于山如玉，及其得于天也，如芝如笋，如鸾如龙，如浙江潮、昆崙楼，又或堂堂也而如人飞空，骋辔以游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319366_comment'></div>昔者山中之人共卧木石之间，安知其至是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319366_comment'></div>至是望焉，欲即之而不可得也，亦可以一怅然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319366_comment'></div>山九真皆秦人，方其避秦也，披榛藿而入，岩栖而涧饮，草衣而木食，欲是堂也得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319366_comment'></div>虽后来为萧为孔为坛为宅不可知，即子真九江弃官变服，亦必飘然为樵夫野人，混混乎其中，其霜露槁乾，岂比茅檐俛仰之适哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319366_comment'></div>而数世之后，仙宫化城，金堂玉室，披华星，佩紫霞，鸣钟列食，波及来者，严严如别馆，不知前八九天人者犹彷佛过之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319366_comment'></div>其高才灵气，第欲如王羲之、陶弘景之流暂游忽别，亦不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319366_comment'></div>何昔之鹑居者望焉而为其所难，而今之舍盖者俨然而不就其所易也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319366_comment'></div>亦可以一怅然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319366_comment'></div>然吾闻古仙人记云，去后千五百年，五陵之间成仙者八百，其时可，其数可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319366_comment'></div>庐陵钟陵不合者如砺，斯堂云海日阅人而如指，安知不有隐君子变姓名而处，岂皆如吾等浅之为信信，又浅之为留题哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319366_comment'></div>咨尔来者，候气审之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319366_comment'></div>旧堂御书楼下如寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319366_comment'></div>提点江西道教、知宫事李允一既修殿馀廊西容焉，高楼广倍，于是副宫许景容分琴书其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319366_comment'></div>允一、景容皆吾州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319366_comment'></div>记成，明月甲子书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1319366_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

茶陵
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7658964fea8f48d9914d0fb08b1f7017_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7658964fea8f48d9914d0fb08b1f7017");'><span id='7658964fea8f48d9914d0fb08b1f7017_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年</a>，65岁</div><div id='7658964fea8f48d9914d0fb08b1f7017' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年</a>　拟游南岳衡山，至茶陵因故返乡。<br /></div>
